	public boolean duplicate(int numbers[],int length,int [] duplication) {
        if(null == numbers || length <= 1){
            return false;
        }
        for (int i = 0; i < length; i++){
            if(numbers[i] != i){
                if(numbers[numbers[i]] == numbers[i]){
                    duplication[0] = numbers[i];
                    return true;
                }else{
                    int temp = numbers[i];
                    numbers[i] = numbers[numbers[i]];
                    numbers[temp] = temp; // æ³¨æ„numbers[i]çš„å€¼å·²æ”¹å˜ï¼Œéœ€è¦ç”¨tempæ¥æŒ‡ä»£åŸnumbers[i]
                }
            }
        }
        return false;
	}

  2. ç¬¬äºŒç§æ€è·¯ï¼šå°† 1~n çš„æ•°å­—ä»ä¸­é—´ m åˆ†ä¸ºä¸¤éƒ¨åˆ†ï¼Œå‰é¢ä¸€åŠä¸º 1~mï¼Œåé¢ä¸€åŠä¸º m+1~nï¼Œå¦‚æœæ•°ç»„ä¸­ 1~m çš„æ•°å­—è¶…è¿‡ m ä¸ªï¼Œåˆ™åœ¨ 1~m ä¸­ä¸€å®šæœ‰é‡å¤çš„æ•°å­—ï¼Œå¦åˆ™ï¼Œåœ¨ m+1~n ä¸­ä¸€å®šæœ‰é‡å¤æ•°å­—ï¼Œè¿™æ ·ç»§ç»­å°†æœ‰é‡å¤æ•°å­—çš„åŒºé—´ä¸€åˆ†ä¸ºäºŒï¼Œç›´åˆ°æ‰¾åˆ°æœ€åçš„æ•°å­—ã€‚

ç¬¬äºŒç§æ€è·¯çš„æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦æ˜¯O(nlogn)ï¼Œç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦æ˜¯O(1)ã€‚ç›¸å½“äºä»¥æ—¶é—´æ¢ç©ºé—´ï¼Œè¿™é‡Œæ¼”ç¤ºç¬¬äºŒç§æ€è·¯ã€‚

	public static boolean duplicate(int numbers[],int length,int [] duplication) {
        return search(numbers, 1, length - 1, duplication);
    }

    private static boolean search(int[] numbers, int begin, int end, int[] duplication){
        while(end >= begin){
            int mid = (begin + end)/2;
            int count = countRange(numbers, begin, mid);
            if(begin == mid){
                if(count > 1){
                    duplication[0] = begin;
                    return true;
                }else{
                    duplication[0] = mid+1;
                    return true;
                }
            }
            if(count > (mid - begin + 1)){
                end = mid;
            }else{
                begin = mid + 1;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

    private static int countRange(int[] numbers, int begin, int end){
        int count = 0;
        for(int i = 0; i < numbers.length; i++){
            if(numbers[i] >= begin && numbers[i] <= end){
                count++;
            }
        }
        return count;
    }

ç»™å®šä¸€ä¸ªäºŒç»´æ•°ç»„ï¼Œå…¶æ¯ä¸€è¡Œä»å·¦åˆ°å³é€’å¢æ’åºï¼Œä»ä¸Šåˆ°ä¸‹ä¹Ÿæ˜¯é€’å¢æ’åºã€‚ç»™å®šä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ï¼Œåˆ¤æ–­è¿™ä¸ªæ•°æ˜¯å¦åœ¨è¯¥äºŒç»´æ•°ç»„ä¸­ã€‚

è®¾ç›®æ ‡æ•°å­—ä¸º targetï¼Œè¯¥äºŒç»´æ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ï¼Œå°äºå®ƒçš„æ•°ä¸€å®šåœ¨å…¶å·¦è¾¹ï¼Œå¤§äºå®ƒçš„æ•°ä¸€å®šåœ¨å…¶ä¸‹è¾¹ã€‚å› æ­¤ï¼Œå¯ä»å³ä¸Šè§’å¼€å§‹æŸ¥æ‰¾ï¼Œè‹¥å³ä¸Šè§’æ•°å­—ç­‰äº targetï¼Œåˆ™æ‰¾åˆ°ï¼›è‹¥å³ä¸Šè§’æ•°å­—å¤§äº targetï¼Œåˆ™target ä¸ä¼šåœ¨è¯¥æ•°å­—å½“å‰åˆ—ä»¥åŠå³è¾¹åˆ—ï¼Œå°†åˆ—æ•°å‡ä¸€ï¼Œä¸‹æ¬¡æœç´¢æ—¶å³ä¸Šè§’å…ƒç´ ä¸ºå½“å‰å…ƒç´ çš„å·¦è¾¹ä¸€ä¸ªä½ç½®ï¼›è‹¥å³ä¸Šè§’æ•°å­—å°äº targetï¼Œåˆ™target ä¸ä¼šåœ¨è¯¥æ•°å­—å½“å‰è¡Œä»¥åŠä¸Šè¾¹åˆ—ï¼Œå°†è¡Œæ•°åŠ ä¸€ï¼Œä¸‹æ¬¡æœç´¢æ—¶å³ä¸Šè§’å…ƒç´ ä¸ºå½“å‰å…ƒç´ çš„ä¸Šè¾¹ä¸€ä¸ªä½ç½®ã€‚è¿™æ ·å°±å¯ä»¥æ ¹æ® target å’Œå½“å‰å…ƒç´ çš„å¤§å°å…³ç³»æ¥ç¼©å°æŸ¥æ‰¾åŒºé—´ï¼Œå½“å‰å…ƒç´ çš„æŸ¥æ‰¾åŒºé—´ä¸ºå·¦ä¸‹è§’çš„æ‰€æœ‰å…ƒç´ ã€‚

ä¹Ÿå¯ä»å·¦ä¸‹è§’å¼€å§‹æŸ¥æ‰¾ï¼Œæ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ O(M + N)ï¼Œç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ O(1)ã€‚å…¶ä¸­ M ä¸ºè¡Œæ•°ï¼ŒN ä¸º åˆ—æ•°ã€‚

Consider the following matrix:
[
  [1,   4,  7, 11, 15],
  [2,   5,  8, 12, 19],
  [3,   6,  9, 16, 22],
  [10, 13, 14, 17, 24],
  [18, 21, 23, 26, 30]
]
 
Given target = 5, return true.
Given target = 20, return false.    
    
	public boolean Find(int target, int [][] array) {
        if(null == array){
            return false;
        }
        int rowBegin = 0;
        int colEnd = array[0].length - 1;
        while(rowBegin <= array.length - 1 && colEnd >= 0){
            if(array[rowBegin][colEnd] == target){
                return true;
            }else if(array[rowBegin][colEnd] > target){
                colEnd--;
            }else{
                rowBegin++;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

  2. æ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ä¸ºO(n)ï¼šå…ˆéå†ä¸€æ¬¡å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œè®¡ç®—å‡ºç©ºæ ¼å­—ç¬¦çš„æ•°é‡ï¼Œæ ¹æ®è¯¥æ•°é‡æ‰©å……åŸå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼ˆæ¯æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªç©ºæ ¼å­—ç¬¦ï¼Œæ‰©å……ä¸¤ä¸ªå­—èŠ‚ï¼‰ã€‚ç”¨ p1 æŒ‡å‘åŸå­—ç¬¦ä¸²å°¾éƒ¨ï¼Œç”¨ p2 æŒ‡å‘æ‰©å……åçš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å°¾éƒ¨ï¼Œå‘å‰ç§»åŠ¨ p1 æŒ‡é’ˆï¼Œå°†å…¶æŒ‡å‘å­—ç¬¦å¤åˆ¶åˆ° p2 æ‰€æŒ‡å‘ä½ç½®ï¼Œp2 ä¹Ÿéšä¹‹ç§»åŠ¨ï¼Œè‹¥è¯¥å­—ç¬¦ä¸ºç©ºæ ¼ï¼Œåˆ™ p2 å¤„åº”è¯¥æ’å…¥ %20ï¼Œç›´è‡³ p1 å’Œ p2 æŒ‡å‘åŒä¸€ä½ç½®ï¼Œè¡¨ç¤ºæ‰€æœ‰ç©ºæ ¼å·²æ›¿æ¢å®Œæ¯•ã€‚

é‡‡ç”¨ç¬¬äºŒç§æ€è·¯ã€‚

ç›¸å…³é¢˜ç›®ï¼š

æœ‰ä¸¤ä¸ªæ’åºæ•°ç»„ A1 å’Œ A2ï¼Œå†…å­˜åœ¨ A1 çš„æœ«å°¾æœ‰è¶³å¤Ÿå¤šçš„ç©ºä½™ç©ºé—´å®¹çº³ A2ã€‚æŠŠ A2 ä¸­æ‰€æœ‰çš„æ•°å­—æ’å…¥ A1ä¸­ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”æ‰€æœ‰çš„æ•°å­—æ˜¯æ’åºçš„ã€‚è¿™é¢˜ä»åå¾€å‰å¤åˆ¶å³å¯ã€‚

Input:
"A B"
 
Output:
"A%20B"

	public String replaceSpace(StringBuffer str) {
        if(null == str){
            return null;
        }else if(str.equals("")){
            return "";
        }
    	int p1 = str.length() - 1;
        for(int i = 0; i <= p1; i++){
            if(str.charAt(i) == ' '){
                str.append("  ");
            }
        }
        int p2 = str.length() - 1;
        while(p1 < p2){
            char temp = str.charAt(p1--);
            if(temp == ' '){
                str.setCharAt(p2--, '0');
                str.setCharAt(p2--, '2');
                str.setCharAt(p2--, '%');
            }else{
                str.setCharAt(p2--, temp);
            }
        }
        return str.toString();
    }

  3. ä¸ç¬¬äºŒç§æ€è·¯ç±»ä¼¼ï¼Œé‡‡ç”¨é€’å½’çš„æ–¹æ³•å®Œæˆä»»åŠ¡ã€‚

*	åè½¬é“¾è¡¨åå†è¾“å‡º

   public ArrayList<Integer> printListFromTailToHead(ListNode listNode) {
       ListNode listNodeHead = new ListNode(-1);
       ListNode temp;
       while(listNode != null){
           temp = listNode.next;
           listNode.next = listNodeHead.next;
           listNodeHead.next = listNode;
           listNode = temp;
       }
       listNode = listNodeHead.next;
       ArrayList<Integer> list = new ArrayList<>();
       while(listNode != null){
           list.add(listNode.val);
           listNode = listNode.next;
       }
       return list;
   }

/**
*	å‹æ ˆæ³•
*/
public ArrayList<Integer> printListFromTailToHead(ListNode listNode) {
       if(null == listNode){
           return null;
       }
       Stack<Integer> stack = new Stack<Integer>();
       while(listNode != null){
           stack.push(listNode.val);
           listNode = listNode.next;
       }
       ArrayList<Integer> list = new ArrayList<Integer>();
       while(!stack.isEmpty()){
           list.add(stack.pop());
       }
       return list;
   }

/**
*	é€’å½’æ³•
*/
   public ArrayList<Integer> printListFromTailToHead(ListNode listNode) {
       ArrayList<Integer> list = new ArrayList<Integer>();
       if(listNode != null){
           list = printListFromTailToHead(listNode.next);
           list.add(listNode.val);
       }
       return list;
   }

åŠ›æ‰£ï¼šç”¨ä¾‹æµ‹è¯•

æ€è·¯åˆ†æï¼š

å‰åºéå†çš„ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°å­—å°±æ˜¯æ ¹èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å€¼ï¼Œå¾—åˆ°è¯¥æ•°å­—åœ¨ä¸­åºéå†çš„ä½ç½®ï¼Œä¸­åºéå†ä¸­ä½äºè¯¥ä½ç½®ä¹‹å‰çš„æ•°å­—éƒ½æ˜¯å·¦å­æ ‘èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å€¼ï¼›ä¸­åºéå†ä¸­ä½äºè¯¥ä½ç½®ä¹‹åçš„æ•°å­—éƒ½æ˜¯å³å­æ ‘èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å€¼ã€‚å†é€’å½’ä»å­æ ‘ä¸­ä¸æ–­æŒ‰ç…§ä¸Šè¿°æ­¥éª¤ç¡®å®šå„å­æ ‘æ ¹èŠ‚ç‚¹ã€‚

private Map<Integer,Integer> map = new HashMap<>();

public TreeNode buildTree(int[] preorder, int[] inorder) {
    for(int i = 0; i < inorder.length; i++){
        map.put(inorder[i],i);
    }
    return buildTreeFunction(preorder, 0, preorder.length - 1, 0);
}

public TreeNode buildTreeFunction(int[] preorder, int preBegin, int preEnd, int in){
    if(preBegin > preEnd){
        return null;
    }
    TreeNode treeNode = new TreeNode(preorder[preBegin]);
    int place = map.get(preorder[preBegin]);
    int leftCount = place - in;
    treeNode.left = buildTreeFunction(preorder, preBegin + 1, preBegin + leftCount, in);
    treeNode.right = buildTreeFunction(preorder, preBegin + leftCount + 1, preEnd, in + leftCount + 1);
    return treeNode;
}

8ã€äºŒå‰æ ‘çš„ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹

é¢˜ç›®ï¼š

ç»™å®šä¸€ä¸ªäºŒå‰æ ‘å’Œå…¶ä¸­çš„ä¸€ä¸ªç»“ç‚¹ï¼Œè¯·æ‰¾å‡ºä¸­åºéå†é¡ºåºçš„ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ªç»“ç‚¹å¹¶ä¸”è¿”å›ã€‚æ³¨æ„ï¼Œæ ‘ä¸­çš„ç»“ç‚¹ä¸ä»…åŒ…å«å·¦å³å­ç»“ç‚¹ï¼ŒåŒæ—¶åŒ…å«æŒ‡å‘çˆ¶ç»“ç‚¹çš„æŒ‡é’ˆã€‚

  2. å¦‚æœä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹æ— å³å­æ ‘ï¼Œä¸”è¯¥èŠ‚ç‚¹ä¸ºå…¶çˆ¶èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å·¦å­èŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆä¸­åºéå†ä¸‹è¿™ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹çš„ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹ä¸ºè¯¥èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„çˆ¶èŠ‚ç‚¹ã€‚
  3. å¦‚æœä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹æ— å³å­æ ‘ï¼Œä¸”è¯¥èŠ‚ç‚¹ä¸ºå…¶çˆ¶èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å³å­èŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆå¯ä»¥æ²¿çˆ¶èŠ‚ç‚¹ä¸€ç›´å‘ä¸Šéå†ï¼Œç›´åˆ°æ‰¾åˆ°æŸä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹ä¸ºå…¶çˆ¶èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å·¦å­èŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆè¯¥èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„çˆ¶èŠ‚ç‚¹å°±ä¸ºæˆ‘ä»¬è¦å¯»æ‰¾çš„èŠ‚ç‚¹ã€‚
  4. ä»¥ä¸Šéƒ½æ²¡æ‰¾åˆ°ï¼Œåˆ™è¯¥èŠ‚ç‚¹ä¸ºè¯¥æ ‘ä¸­åºéå†çš„æœ€åä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹ã€‚
public TreeLinkNode GetNext(TreeLinkNode pNode){
    if(pNode == null){
        return null;
    }
    if(pNode.right != null){
        pNode = pNode.right;
        while(pNode.left != null){
            pNode = pNode.left;
        }
        return pNode;
    }else{
        while(pNode.next != null){
            if(pNode.next.left == pNode){
                return pNode.next;
            }else{
                pNode = pNode.next;
            }
        }
    }
    return null;
}

public class Solution {
    Stack<Integer> stack1 = new Stack<Integer>();
    Stack<Integer> stack2 = new Stack<Integer>();
    
    public void push(int node) {
        stack1.push(node);
    }
    
    public int pop() {
        if(stack2.isEmpty()){
            while(!stack1.isEmpty()){
                stack2.push(stack1.pop());
            }
        }
        if(stack2.isEmpty()){
            throw new RuntimeException("Queue is empty!");
        }
        return stack2.pop();
    }
}

public int Fibonacci(int n) {
    if(n <= 1){
        return n;
    }
    int fb0 = 0;
    int fb1 = 1;
    int ans = 0;
    for(int i = 2; i <= n; i++){
        ans = fb0 + fb1;
        fb0 = fb1;
        fb1 = ans;
    }
    return ans;
}

    Â· ç‰¹æ®Šæƒ…å†µ2ï¼šæ•°ç»„ä¸­æ•°å­—é‡å¤ï¼Œä¸‰ä¸ªæŒ‡é’ˆæŒ‡å‘å…ƒç´ ç›¸ç­‰ï¼Œæ— æ³•åˆ¤æ–­ç¬¬ä¸‰ä¸ªæŒ‡é’ˆæŒ‡å‘å…ƒç´ å±äºå“ªä¸ªæ•°ç»„ï¼Œè¿™æ—¶åªèƒ½ç”¨é¡ºåºæŸ¥æ‰¾æ³•ã€‚

è¿™é‡Œé‡‡ç”¨ç¬¬äºŒç§æ€è·¯ã€‚

public int minNumberInRotateArray(int [] array) {
    if(null == array || array.length <= 0){
        throw new RuntimeException("Invalid array!");
    }
    int begin = 0;
    int end = array.length - 1;
    int mid = begin; //åˆå§‹åŒ–beginï¼Œå¯ä»¥åœ¨æœªæ—‹è½¬çš„è¿™ç§ç‰¹æ®Šæƒ…å†µä¸‹ï¼Œç›´æ¥è¾“å‡ºç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå…ƒç´ ï¼Œä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯æœ€å°çš„å…ƒç´ 
    while(array[begin] >= array[end]){
        if(end - begin == 1){
            return array[end];
        }
        if(array[begin] == array[end] && array[begin] == array[mid]){
            return minNum(array, begin, end);
        }
        mid = (begin + end) / 2;
        if(array[mid] >= array[begin]){
            begin = mid;
        }else if(array[mid] <= array[end]){
            end = mid;
        }
    }
    return array[end];
}

private int minNum(int [] array, int begin, int end){
    int res = array[begin];
    for(int i = begin + 1; i <= end; i++){
        if(res > array[i]){
            res = array[i];
        }
    }
    return res;
}

12ã€çŸ©é˜µä¸­çš„è·¯å¾„

é¢˜ç›®ï¼š

åˆ¤æ–­åœ¨ä¸€ä¸ªçŸ©é˜µä¸­æ˜¯å¦å­˜åœ¨ä¸€æ¡åŒ…å«æŸå­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ‰€æœ‰å­—ç¬¦çš„è·¯å¾„ã€‚è·¯å¾„å¯ä»¥ä»çŸ©é˜µä¸­çš„ä»»æ„ä¸€ä¸ªæ ¼å­å¼€å§‹ï¼Œæ¯ä¸€æ­¥å¯ä»¥åœ¨çŸ©é˜µä¸­å‘ä¸Šä¸‹å·¦å³ç§»åŠ¨ä¸€ä¸ªæ ¼å­ã€‚å¦‚æœä¸€æ¡è·¯å¾„ç»è¿‡äº†çŸ©é˜µä¸­çš„æŸä¸€ä¸ªæ ¼å­ï¼Œåˆ™è¯¥è·¯å¾„ä¸èƒ½å†è¿›å…¥è¯¥æ ¼å­ã€‚ä¾‹å¦‚ä¸‹é¢çš„çŸ©é˜µåŒ…å«äº†ä¸€æ¡ bfce è·¯å¾„ã€‚

ç‰›å®¢ç½‘ï¼šç”¨ä¾‹æµ‹è¯•

æ€è·¯åˆ†æï¼š

ç›´æ¥é‡‡ç”¨å›æº¯æ³•ï¼Œéå†èµ·ç‚¹ä½ç½®ï¼Œç„¶åæŒ‰ç…§ä¸Šä¸‹å·¦å³çš„é¡ºåºè¿›è¡Œé€’å½’ã€‚

public boolean hasPath(char[] matrix, int rows, int cols, char[] str){
    if(null == matrix || rows <= 0 || cols <= 0){
        return false;
    }
    char[][] buildedMatrix = buildMatrix(matrix, rows, cols);
    boolean[][] marked = new boolean[rows][cols];
    for(int i = 0; i < rows; i++){
        for(int j = 0; j < cols; j++){
            if(findWay(buildedMatrix, rows, cols, i, j, str, marked, 0)){
                return true;
            }
        }
    }
    return false;
}

/**
*    å›æº¯æ³•å¯»æ‰¾
*/
private boolean findWay(char[][] buildedMatrix, int rows, int cols, int row, int col, char[] str, boolean[][] marked, int point){
    if(point == str.length){ //å…ˆåˆ¤æ–­è¿™ä¸ªæ¡ä»¶ï¼Œé¿å…ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ªåˆ¤æ–­å‡ºç°æ•°ç»„ç´¢å¼•å¼‚å¸¸
        return true;
    }
    if(row < 0 || row >= rows || col < 0 || col >= cols 
       || marked[row][col] == true || str[point] != buildedMatrix[row][col]){ //æ³¨æ„è¦å…ˆåˆ¤æ–­rowå’Œcolæœ‰æ²¡æœ‰è¶Šç•Œï¼Œä¸ç„¶ä¼šå‡ºç°æ•°ç»„ç´¢å¼•å¼‚å¸¸
        return false;
    }
    marked[row][col] = true;
    if(findWay(buildedMatrix, rows, cols, row - 1, col, str, marked, point + 1)){ // ä¸Š
        return true;
    }
    if(findWay(buildedMatrix, rows, cols, row + 1, col, str, marked, point + 1)){ // ä¸‹
        return true;
    }
    if(findWay(buildedMatrix, rows, cols, row, col - 1, str, marked, point + 1)){ // å·¦
        return true;
    }
    if(findWay(buildedMatrix, rows, cols, row, col + 1, str, marked, point + 1)){ // å³
        return true;
    }
    marked[row][col] = false;
    return false;
}

/**
*    å°†è¾“å…¥çš„ä¸€ç»´æ•°ç»„è½¬æ¢ä¸ºé—®é¢˜æ‰€æè¿°çš„çŸ©é˜µ
*/
private char[][] buildMatrix(char[] matrix, int rows, int cols){
    char[][] buildedMatrix = new char[rows][cols];
    for(int i = 0; i < rows; i++){
        for(int j = 0; j < cols; j++){
            buildedMatrix[i][j] = matrix[cols * i + j];
        }
    }
    return buildedMatrix;
}

private int cnt = 0;

public int movingCount(int threshold, int rows, int cols){
    if(threshold < 0 || rows < 0 || cols < 0){
        return 0;
    }
    boolean[][] marked = new boolean[rows][cols];
    move(marked, threshold, rows, cols, 0, 0);
    return cnt;
}

private void move(boolean[][] marked, int threshold, int rows, int cols, int row, int col){
    if(col < 0 || col >= cols || row < 0 || row >= rows || marked[row][col] == true || calSum(row, col) > threshold){
        return;
    }
    cnt++;
    marked[row][col] = true;
    move(marked, threshold, rows, cols, row - 1, col);
    move(marked, threshold, rows, cols, row + 1, col);
    move(marked, threshold, rows, cols, row, col - 1);
    move(marked, threshold, rows, cols, row, col + 1);
}

private int calSum(int row, int col){
    int sum = 0;
    while(row % 10 != 0){
        sum = sum + row % 10;
        row = row / 10;
    }
    while(col % 10 != 0){
        sum = sum + col % 10;
        col = col / 10;
    }
    return sum;

   /**
   *	åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’æ³•
   */
public int cutRope(int target) {
       if(target < 2){
           return 0;
       }else if(target == 2){
           return 1;
       }else if(target == 3){
           return 2;
       }
       int[] profit = new int[target + 1];
       profit[0] = 0;
       profit[1] = 1;
       profit[2] = 2;
       profit[3] = 3;
       int max = 0;
       for(int i = 4; i <= target; i++){
           max = 0;
           for(int j = 1; j <= i / 2; j++){
               if(max < profit[j] * profit[i - j]){
                   max = profit[j] * profit[i - j];
               }
           }
           profit[i] = max;
       }
       return profit[target];
   }

/**
*	è´ªå©ªç®—æ³•
*/
   public int cutRope(int target) {
       if(target < 2){
           return 0;
       }else if(target == 2){
           return 1;
       }else if(target == 3){
           return 2;
       }
       int num_3 = target / 3;
       if(target % 3 == 1){
           num_3--;
           return 2 * 2 * (int)Math.pow(3, num_3);
       }
       return ((target % 3) == 0 ? 1 : 2) * (int)Math.pow(3, num_3);
   }

public int NumberOf1(int n) {
       int helper = 1;
       int count = 0;
       while(helper != 0){
           if((n & helper) != 0){
               count++;
           }
           helper = helper << 1;
       }
       return count;
   }

/**
*	æ–¹æ³•2
*/
public int NumberOf1(int n) {
       int count = 0;
       while(n != 0){
           count++;
           n = n & (n - 1);
       }
       return count;
   }

  public double Power(double base, int exponent) {
      double res;
      if(base == 0){
          return 0;
      }
      if(exponent < 0){
          return 1.0 / calPower(base, -exponent);
      }else{
          return calPower(base, exponent);
      }
}
  
  private double calPower(double base, int exponent){
      if(exponent == 0){
          return 1;
      }
      if(exponent == 1){
          return base;
      }
      double res = calPower(base, exponent >> 1);
      res = res * res;
      if((exponent & 1) != 0){
          res = res * base;
      }
      return res;
  }

private static void print1ToMax(int length){
        if(length <= 0){
            return;
        }else {
            char[] c = new char[length];
            for(int i = 0; i < length; i++){
                c[i] = '0';
            }
            print1ToMaxRecursively(c, length, 0);
        }
    }

    private static void print1ToMaxRecursively(char[] c, int length, int index){
        if(index == length){
            printNum(c);
            return;
        }
        for(int i = 0; i < 10; i++){
            c[index] = (char)(i+48);
            print1ToMaxRecursively(c, length, index + 1);
        }
    }

    private static void printNum(char[] c){
        boolean flag = false;
        for(int i = 0; i < c.length; i++){
            if(c[i] != '0' && flag == false){
                flag = true;
            }
            if(flag){
                System.out.print(c[i]);
            }
        }
        if(flag){
            System.out.println();
        }
    }

  1. è¾“å…¥ä¸º nullï¼›
  2. é“¾è¡¨åªæœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œåˆ é™¤è¯¥èŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼›
  3. é“¾è¡¨ä¸åªæœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œåˆ é™¤å°¾èŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œè¿™æ—¶è¿˜æ˜¯è¦å¾ªç¯æ‰¾åˆ°éœ€è¦çš„èŠ‚ç‚¹ã€‚
public ListNode deleteNode(ListNode head, ListNode tobeDelete) {
    if(head == null || tobeDelete == null){
        return null;
    }
    if(tobeDelete.next != null){
        tobeDelete.val = tobeDelete.next.val;
        tobeDelete.next = tobeDelete.next.next;
    }else if(head.next == null){
        head = null;
    }else{
        ListNode temp = head;
        while(temp.next != tobeDelete){
            temp = temp.next;
        }
        temp.next = null;
    }
    return head;
}

é¢˜ç›®ï¼š

åœ¨ä¸€ä¸ªæ’åºçš„é“¾è¡¨ä¸­ï¼Œå­˜åœ¨é‡å¤çš„ç»“ç‚¹ï¼Œè¯·åˆ é™¤è¯¥é“¾è¡¨ä¸­é‡å¤çš„ç»“ç‚¹ï¼Œé‡å¤çš„ç»“ç‚¹ä¸ä¿ç•™ï¼Œè¿”å›é“¾è¡¨å¤´æŒ‡é’ˆã€‚ ä¾‹å¦‚ï¼Œé“¾è¡¨1->2->3->3->4->4->5 å¤„ç†åä¸º 1->2->5ã€‚

public ListNode deleteDuplication(ListNode pHead)
{
    if(pHead == null || pHead.next == null){
        return pHead;
    }
    while(pHead.next != null && pHead.val == pHead.next.val){
        while(pHead.next != null && pHead.val == pHead.next.val){
            pHead = pHead.next;
        }
        if(pHead.next == null){
            return null;
        }
        pHead = pHead.next;
    }
    ListNode preNode = pHead;
    ListNode temp = pHead.next;
    while(temp != null && temp.next != null){
        if(temp.next != null && temp.val == temp.next.val){
            while(temp.next != null && temp.val == temp.next.val){
                temp = temp.next;
            }
            preNode.next = temp.next;
            temp = temp.next;
        }else{
            temp = temp.next;
            preNode = preNode.next; 
        }
    }
    return pHead;
}

  1. è‹¥ p.charAt( j ) ä¸º â€˜ . â€™ æˆ–è€…ä¸ s.charAt( i ) ç›¸ç­‰ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆdp[ i+1 ] [ j+1 ] = dp[ i ] [ j ]ï¼›
  2. è‹¥ p.charAt( j ) ä¸º â€˜ * â€™ï¼šè‹¥p.charAt(j - 1) != s.charAt(i) && p.charAt(j - 1) != â€˜.â€™ï¼Œåˆ™ x*åº”ç›¸å½“äºä¸ºç©ºï¼›p çš„å½“å‰å­—ç¬¦çš„å‰ä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦èƒ½ä¸ s å½“å‰å­—ç¬¦åŒ¹é…ä¸Šï¼Œåˆ™æœ‰ä¸‰ç§æƒ…å†µï¼š1.x*ç›¸å½“äºä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ã€‚2.x*ç›¸å½“äºå¤šä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ã€‚3.x*ç›¸å½“äºç©ºã€‚
  3. æ³¨æ„éœ€è¦åˆå§‹åŒ–ä»¥åŠé˜²æ­¢æ•°ç»„ç´¢å¼•å°äº0ã€‚
public boolean isMatch(String s, String p) {
    if(s == null || p == null){
        return false;
    }
    boolean[][] dp = new boolean[s.length() + 1][p.length() + 1];
    dp[0][0] = true;
    for(int i = 1; i < p.length(); i++){ //"aab"  "c*a*b"
        if(p.charAt(i) == '*' && dp[0][i - 1]){
            dp[0][i + 1] = true;
        }
    }
    for(int i = 0; i < s.length(); i++){
        for(int j = 0; j < p.length(); j++){
            if(s.charAt(i) == p.charAt(j) || p.charAt(j) == '.'){
                dp[i + 1][j + 1] = dp[i][j];
            }else if(j > 0 && p.charAt(j) == '*'){
                if(p.charAt(j - 1) != s.charAt(i) && p.charAt(j - 1) != '.'){
                    dp[i + 1][j + 1] = dp[i + 1][j - 1];
                }else{
                    dp[i + 1][j + 1] = (dp[i + 1][j] || dp[i][j + 1] || dp[i + 1][j - 1]);
                }
            }
        }
    }
    return dp[s.length()][p.length()];
}

è¯·å®ç°ä¸€ä¸ªå‡½æ•°ç”¨æ¥åˆ¤æ–­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ˜¯å¦è¡¨ç¤ºæ•°å€¼ï¼ˆåŒ…æ‹¬æ•´æ•°å’Œå°æ•°ï¼‰ã€‚ä¾‹å¦‚ï¼Œå­—ç¬¦ä¸²"+100"ã€â€œ5e2â€ã€"-123"ã€â€œ3.1416â€ã€â€œ0123"éƒ½è¡¨ç¤ºæ•°å€¼ï¼Œä½†"12eâ€ã€â€œ1a3.14â€ã€â€œ1.2.3â€ã€â€œÂ±5â€ã€"-1E-16"åŠ"12e+5.4"éƒ½ä¸æ˜¯ã€‚

public boolean isNumber(String s) {
    if(s == null){
        return false;
    }
    int index = 0;
    //è·³è¿‡å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æœ€å¼€å§‹çš„ç©ºæ ¼
    while(index < s.length() && s.charAt(index) == ' '){
        index++;
    }
    //å¦‚æœåªæœ‰ç©ºæ ¼ï¼Œfalse
    if(index == s.length()){
        return false;
    }
    // dotå°æ•°çš„ä¸ªæ•°ï¼Œnumæ•°å­—çš„ä¸ªæ•°ï¼ŒeæŒ‡æ•°ç¬¦å·çš„ä¸ªæ•°
    int dot = 0, num = 0, e = 0;
    //å‡ºç°æ­£è´Ÿå·ï¼Œå®ƒä»¬çš„åé¢ä¸€ä¸ªä¸èƒ½å†æ˜¯æ­£è´Ÿå·ï¼Œä¸èƒ½åé¢æ— å…ƒç´ 
    if(s.charAt(index) == '-' || s.charAt(index) == '+'){
        index++;
        if(index == s.length()){
            return false;
        }
        if(s.charAt(index) == '-' || s.charAt(index) == '+'){
            return false;
        }
    }
    while(index < s.length()){
        if(s.charAt(index) >= '0' && s.charAt(index) <= '9'){
            num++;
            index++;
            //å‡ºç°å°æ•°ç‚¹ï¼Œåªèƒ½æœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªå°æ•°ç‚¹ï¼Œä¸”åœ¨è¿™ä¹‹å‰ä¸èƒ½æœ‰e
        }else if(s.charAt(index) == '.'){
            if(dot > 0 || e > 0){
                return false;
            }
            //é˜²æ­¢â€œ.â€è¿™ç§ç°è±¡å‘ç”Ÿ
            if(num == 0 && ((index + 1) == s.length() || s.charAt(index + 1) < '0' || s.charAt(index + 1) > '9')){
                return false;
            }
            dot++;
            index++;
            //å‡ºç°eï¼Œeçš„å‰é¢ä¸èƒ½ä¸å‡ºç°æ•°å­—ï¼Œä¸”åªèƒ½å‡ºç°ä¸€æ¬¡eï¼Œeçš„åé¢å¦‚æœæ˜¯æ­£è´Ÿå·ï¼Œéœ€è¦åƒä¸Šé¢ä¸€æ ·åˆ¤æ–­ï¼Œå¦‚æœeçš„åé¢æ— å…ƒç´ ï¼Œå³æ— å…ƒç´ æˆ–è€…æ˜¯ç©ºæ ¼ï¼Œä¹Ÿæ˜¯ä¸è¡Œçš„
        }else if(s.charAt(index) == 'e' || s.charAt(index) == 'E'){
            if(num == 0 || e > 0){
                return false;
            }
            e++;
            index++;
            if(index < s.length() && (s.charAt(index) == '-' || s.charAt(index) == '+')){
                index++;
                if(index == s.length()){
                    return false;
                }
                if(s.charAt(index) == '-' || s.charAt(index) == '+'){
                    return false;
                }
            }
            if(index == s.length() || s.charAt(index) == ' '){
                return false;
            }
            //å»æ‰ç»“å°¾çš„ç©ºæ ¼
        }else if(s.charAt(index) == ' '){
            if(num == 0){
                return false;
            }
            while(index < s.length()){
                if(s.charAt(index) != ' '){
                    return false;
                }
                index++;
            }
        }else{
            return false;
        }
    }
    return true;
}

è¾“å…¥ä¸€ä¸ªæ•´æ•°æ•°ç»„ï¼Œå®ç°ä¸€ä¸ªå‡½æ•°æ¥è°ƒæ•´è¯¥æ•°ç»„ä¸­æ•°å­—çš„é¡ºåºï¼Œä½¿å¾—æ‰€æœ‰å¥‡æ•°ä½äºæ•°ç»„çš„å‰åŠéƒ¨åˆ†ï¼Œæ‰€æœ‰å¶æ•°ä½äºæ•°ç»„çš„ååŠéƒ¨åˆ†ã€‚

é‡‡ç”¨åŒæŒ‡é’ˆï¼Œä¸€ä¸ªæŒ‡å‘æ•°ç»„å¤´ï¼Œä¸€ä¸ªæŒ‡å‘æ•°ç»„å°¾ï¼Œå‘ä¸­é—´é€’è¿›ã€‚è‹¥ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªæŒ‡é’ˆå‘ç°å¶æ•°ï¼Œç¬¬äºŒä¸ªæŒ‡é’ˆå‘ç°å¥‡æ•°ï¼Œåˆ™è°ƒæ¢å®ƒä»¬çš„é¡ºåºã€‚è¿˜å¯é‡‡ç”¨å†’æ³¡æ³•ï¼Œæˆ–è€…å¤åˆ¶ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ï¼Œå…ˆå°†æ•°ç»„å¥‡å¶ä¸ªæ•°æ±‚å‡ºæ¥ï¼Œå†éå†æ•°ç»„å°†æ¯ä¸ªæ•°å­—æ”¾åˆ°åˆé€‚çš„ç±»åˆ«ä¸­ã€‚æ³¨æ„ï¼Œè¿™é‡Œä¹¦ä¸­æåˆ°å¯ä»¥å¢åŠ ç¨‹åºçš„æ‰©å±•æ€§ï¼Œå³æœªæ¥ä¸åªæ˜¯åˆ†å¼€å¥‡å¶æ•°ï¼Œä¹Ÿå¯ä»¥æœ‰åˆ«çš„åŠŸèƒ½ï¼Œè¿™å¯ä»¥å°†åˆ¤æ–­å‡½æ•°åŠ å…¥è¿›å½¢å‚ä¸­ï¼Œè¿™æ ·å°±å¢åŠ äº†ç¨‹åºçš„æ‰©å±•æ€§ã€‚

public int[] exchange(int[] nums) {
    if(nums == null || nums.length <= 1){
        return nums;
    }
    int begin = 0;
    int end = nums.length - 1;
    while(begin < end){
        while(end > begin && (nums[end] & 1) == 0){
            end--;
        }
        while(end > begin  && (nums[begin] & 1) != 0){
            begin++;
        }
        int temp = nums[begin];
        nums[begin] = nums[end];
        nums[end] = temp;
    }
    return nums;
}

public ListNode getKthFromEnd(ListNode head, int k) {
    if(head == null || k <= 0){
        return null;
    }
    ListNode begin  = head;
    for(int i = 0; i < k - 1; i++){
        if(begin != null){
            begin = begin.next;
        }else{
            return null;
        }
    }
    ListNode target = head;
    while(begin.next != null){
        begin = begin.next;
        target = target.next;
    }
    return target;
}

  1. ç›¸é‡èŠ‚ç‚¹å¤„ï¼Œå¾—åˆ°ç›¸é‡èŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œé€šè¿‡è¯¥èŠ‚ç‚¹å¯ä»¥å¾—åˆ°ç¯çš„é•¿åº¦ã€‚å†åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸¤ä¸ªæŒ‡é’ˆï¼Œä»å¤´èŠ‚ç‚¹å¼€å§‹ï¼Œä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹å…ˆèµ°ç¯çš„é•¿åº¦çš„æ­¥æ•°ã€‚ä»è¿™ä¹‹åï¼Œä¸¤ä¸ªæŒ‡é’ˆæ¯æ¬¡èµ° 1 æ­¥ï¼Œå®ƒä»¬çš„ç›¸é‡èŠ‚ç‚¹å³ä¸ºç¯å…¥å£èŠ‚ç‚¹ã€‚
  2. ç›¸é‡èŠ‚ç‚¹å¤„ï¼Œå¾—åˆ°ç›¸é‡èŠ‚ç‚¹ã€‚å°†å¿«çš„æŒ‡é’ˆé‡ç½®ä¸ºå¤´èŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œè®©ä¸¤ä¸ªæŒ‡é’ˆæ¯æ¬¡èµ°ä¸€æ­¥ï¼Œä¸¤æŒ‡é’ˆç›¸é‡èŠ‚ç‚¹å³ä¸ºç¯å…¥å£èŠ‚ç‚¹ã€‚
public ListNode EntryNodeOfLoop(ListNode pHead)
{
    if(pHead == null){
        return null;
    }
    ListNode p1 = pHead; //å¿«çš„æŒ‡é’ˆ
    ListNode p2 = pHead; //æ…¢çš„æŒ‡é’ˆ
    while(p1 != null && p1.next !=null){
        p1 = p1.next.next;
        p2 = p2.next;
        if(p1 == p2){
            break;
        }
    }
    if(p1 == null || p1.next == null){
        return null;
    }else{
        p1 = pHead;
        while(p1 != p2){
            p1 = p1.next;
            p2 = p2.next;
        }
    }
    return p1;
}

   public ListNode reverseList(ListNode head) {
       if(head == null || head.next == null){
           return head;
       }
       ListNode node = head.next;
       head.next = null;
       ListNode newList = reverseList(node);
       node.next = head;
       return newList;
   }

/**
*	å¤´æ’æ³•
*/
public ListNode reverseList(ListNode head) {
       if(head == null || head.next == null){
           return head;
       }
       ListNode newList = new ListNode(-1);
       ListNode tempOriginal = head;
       ListNode temp = null;
       while(tempOriginal != null){
           temp = tempOriginal.next;
           tempOriginal.next = newList.next;
           newList.next = tempOriginal;
           tempOriginal = temp;
       }
       return newList.next;
   }

   */
public ListNode mergeTwoLists(ListNode l1, ListNode l2) {
       if(l1 == null){
           return l2;
       }else if(l2 == null){
           return l1;
       }
       ListNode newHead= null;
       if(l1.val <= l2.val){
           newHead = l1;
           newHead.next = mergeTwoLists(l1.next, l2);
       }else{
           newHead = l2;
           newHead.next = mergeTwoLists(l1, l2.next);
       }
       return newHead;
   }

/**
*	è¿­ä»£æ³•ï¼Œæ³¨æ„è¿™é‡Œè¾¹ç•Œæ¡ä»¶åœ¨åé¢ä¹Ÿåšäº†ä¸€æ¬¡åˆ¤æ–­ï¼Œå› æ­¤ä¸éœ€è¦åœ¨å¼€å¤´è¿›è¡Œè¾¹ç•Œæ¡ä»¶çš„åˆ¤æ–­
*/
public ListNode mergeTwoLists(ListNode l1, ListNode l2) {
       ListNode newHead = new ListNode(-1);
       ListNode temp = newHead;
       while(l1 != null && l2 != null){
           if(l1.val <= l2.val){
               temp.next = l1;
               l1 = l1.next;
           }else{
               temp.next = l2;
               l2 = l2.next;
           }
           temp = temp.next;
       }
       if(l1 == null){
           temp.next = l2;
       }else if(l2 == null){
           temp.next = l1;
       }
       return newHead.next;

   }

Bæ˜¯Açš„å­ç»“æ„ï¼Œ å³ Aä¸­æœ‰å‡ºç°å’ŒBç›¸åŒçš„ç»“æ„å’ŒèŠ‚ç‚¹å€¼ã€‚

public boolean isSubStructure(TreeNode A, TreeNode B) {
    if(A == null || B == null){
        return false;
    }
    return isSubStructure2(A, B) || isSubStructure(A.left, B) || isSubStructure(A.right, B);
}

private boolean isSubStructure2(TreeNode A, TreeNode B){
    if(B == null){
        return true;
    }
    if(A == null){
        return false;
    }
    if(A.val != B.val){
        return false;
    }
    return isSubStructure2(A.left, B.left) && isSubStructure2(A.right, B.right);
}

public TreeNode mirrorTree(TreeNode root) {
    mirrorTreeRecursively(root);
    return root;
}


private void mirrorTreeRecursively(TreeNode node){
    if(node == null){
        return;
    }
    TreeNode temp = node.left;
    node.left = node.right;
    node.right = temp;
    mirrorTreeRecursively(node.left);
    mirrorTreeRecursively(node.right);
}

28ã€å¯¹ç§°çš„äºŒå‰æ ‘

è¯·å®ç°ä¸€ä¸ªå‡½æ•°ï¼Œç”¨æ¥åˆ¤æ–­ä¸€æ£µäºŒå‰æ ‘æ˜¯ä¸æ˜¯å¯¹ç§°çš„ã€‚å¦‚æœä¸€æ£µäºŒå‰æ ‘å’Œå®ƒçš„é•œåƒä¸€æ ·ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆå®ƒæ˜¯å¯¹ç§°çš„ã€‚

public boolean isSymmetric(TreeNode root) {
    return isSymmetric(root, root);
}

private boolean isSymmetric(TreeNode node1, TreeNode node2){
    if(node1 == null && node2 == null){
        return true;
    }
    if(node1 == null || node2 == null){
        return false;
    }
    if(node1.val == node2.val){
        return isSymmetric(node1.left, node2.right) && isSymmetric(node1.right, node2.left);
    }
    return false;
}

  3. åœ¨ç»ˆç‚¹è¡Œï¼Œä»ç»ˆç‚¹åˆ—éå†è‡³èµ·ç‚¹åˆ—ï¼Œç›¸å½“äºä»å³åˆ°å·¦ï¼Œå®Œæˆåç»ˆç‚¹è¡Œå‡ä¸€ï¼Œè‹¥ç»ˆç‚¹è¡Œå°äºèµ·ç‚¹è¡Œï¼Œåˆ™å®Œæˆä»»åŠ¡ï¼›
  4. åœ¨èµ·ç‚¹åˆ—ï¼Œä»ç»ˆç‚¹è¡Œéå†è‡³èµ·ç‚¹è¡Œï¼Œç›¸å½“äºä»ä¸‹åˆ°ä¸Šï¼Œå®Œæˆåèµ·ç‚¹åˆ—åŠ ä¸€ï¼Œè‹¥èµ·ç‚¹åˆ—å¤§äºç»ˆç‚¹åˆ—ï¼Œåˆ™å®Œæˆä»»åŠ¡ã€‚
public int[] spiralOrder(int[][] matrix) {
    if(matrix == null){
        return null;
    }
    if(matrix.length == 0){
        return new int[0];
    }
    int row = matrix.length - 1;
    int col = matrix[0].length - 1;
    int r = 0, c = 0;
    int[] array = new int[(row + 1) * (col + 1)];
    int index = 0;
    while(true){
        for(int i = c; i <= col; i++){
            array[index] = matrix[r][i];
            index++;
        }
        if(++r > row){
            break;
        }
        for(int i = r; i <= row; i++){
            array[index] = matrix[i][col];
            index++;
        }
        if(--col < c){
            break;
        }
        for(int i = col; i >= c; i--){
            array[index] = matrix[row][i];
            index++;
        }
        if(--row < r){
            break;
        }
        for(int i = row; i >= r; i--){
            array[index] = matrix[i][c];
            index++;
        }
        if(++c > col){
            break;
        }
    }
    return array;
}

private Stack<Integer> data = new Stack<>();
private Stack<Integer> min = new Stack<>();
public MinStack() {

}

public void push(int x) {
    data.push(x);
    if(min.isEmpty() || x < min.peek()){
        min.push(x);
    }else{
        min.push(min.peek());
    }
}

public void pop() {
    data.pop();
    min.pop();
}

public int top() {
    return data.peek();
}

public int min() {
    return min.peek();
}

31ã€æ ˆçš„å‹å…¥ã€å¼¹å‡ºåºåˆ—

é¢˜ç›®ï¼š

è¾“å…¥ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•´æ•°åºåˆ—ï¼Œç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªåºåˆ—è¡¨ç¤ºæ ˆçš„å‹å…¥é¡ºåºï¼Œè¯·åˆ¤æ–­ç¬¬äºŒä¸ªåºåˆ—æ˜¯å¦ä¸ºè¯¥æ ˆçš„å¼¹å‡ºé¡ºåºã€‚å‡è®¾å‹å…¥æ ˆçš„æ‰€æœ‰æ•°å­—å‡ä¸ç›¸ç­‰ã€‚ä¾‹å¦‚ï¼Œåºåˆ— {1,2,3,4,5} æ˜¯æŸæ ˆçš„å‹æ ˆåºåˆ—ï¼Œåºåˆ— {4,5,3,2,1} æ˜¯è¯¥å‹æ ˆåºåˆ—å¯¹åº”çš„ä¸€ä¸ªå¼¹å‡ºåºåˆ—ï¼Œä½† {4,3,5,1,2} å°±ä¸å¯èƒ½æ˜¯è¯¥å‹æ ˆåºåˆ—çš„å¼¹å‡ºåºåˆ—ã€‚

å®šä¹‰ä¸€ä¸ªè¾…åŠ©æ ˆï¼Œå¦‚æœä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ªè¦å¼¹å‡ºçš„æ•°å­—åˆšå¥½æ˜¯æ ˆé¡¶å…ƒç´ ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆç›´æ¥å¼¹å‡ºï¼›å¦‚æœä¸æ˜¯ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆæŠŠå‹æ ˆåºåˆ—å‰©ä½™çš„æ•°å­—ä¾æ¬¡å‹å…¥è¾…åŠ©æ ˆä¸­ï¼Œç›´è‡³æ‰¾åˆ°éœ€è¦å¼¹å‡ºçš„æ•°å­—ï¼Œè‹¥æ‰€æœ‰æ•°å­—éƒ½å‹å…¥æ ˆä¸­åä»ç„¶æœªæ‰¾åˆ°è¯¥æ•°å­—ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆè¯¥åºåˆ—ä¸ä¸ºå¼¹å‡ºåºåˆ—ã€‚

public boolean validateStackSequences(int[] pushed, int[] popped) {
    if(pushed == null || popped == null){
        return false;
    }
    if((pushed.length == 0 && popped.length != 0) || (pushed.length != 0 && popped.length == 0)){
        return false;
    }
    int indexPush = 0;
    int indexPop = 0;
    Stack<Integer> stack = new Stack<>();
    while(indexPop < popped.length){
        while(stack.isEmpty() || stack.peek() != popped[indexPop]){
            if(indexPush >= pushed.length){
                return false;
            }
            stack.push(pushed[indexPush++]);
        }
        stack.pop();
        indexPop++;
    }
    return true;
}

32.1ã€ä»ä¸Šåˆ°ä¸‹æ‰“å°äºŒå‰æ ‘

é¢˜ç›®ï¼š

ä»ä¸Šåˆ°ä¸‹æ‰“å°å‡ºäºŒå‰æ ‘çš„æ¯ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼ŒåŒä¸€å±‚çš„èŠ‚ç‚¹æŒ‰ç…§ä»å·¦åˆ°å³çš„é¡ºåºæ‰“å°ã€‚

åŠ›æ‰£ï¼šç”¨ä¾‹æµ‹è¯•

æ€è·¯åˆ†æï¼š

å°†èŠ‚ç‚¹ä¿å­˜åˆ°å®¹å™¨ä¸­ã€‚æ¯ç»è¿‡ä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œå¼¹å‡ºå®¹å™¨ä¸­çš„è¯¥èŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œå¹¶å°†è¯¥èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å·¦å³å­èŠ‚ç‚¹ä¿å­˜åˆ°è¯¥å®¹å™¨å°¾å·´å¤„ã€‚éå†è¯¥å®¹å™¨ã€‚

public int[] levelOrder(TreeNode root) {
    if(root == null){
        return new int[0];
    }
    Queue<TreeNode> queue = new LinkedList<>();
    ArrayList<Integer> arrayList = new ArrayList<>();
    queue.add(root);
    arrayList.add(root.val);
    while(queue.size() != 0){
        TreeNode treeNode = queue.poll();
        if(treeNode.left != null){
            queue.add(treeNode.left);
            arrayList.add(treeNode.left.val);
        }
        if(treeNode.right != null){
            queue.add(treeNode.right);
            arrayList.add(treeNode.right.val);
        }
    }
    int[] res = new int[arrayList.size()];
    int index = 0;
    for(Integer i : arrayList){
        res[index++] = i;
    }
    return res;
}

32.2 åˆ†è¡Œä»ä¸Šåˆ°ä¸‹æ‰“å°äºŒå‰æ ‘

é¢˜ç›®ï¼š

ä»ä¸Šåˆ°ä¸‹æŒ‰å±‚æ‰“å°äºŒå‰æ ‘ï¼ŒåŒä¸€å±‚çš„èŠ‚ç‚¹æŒ‰ä»å·¦åˆ°å³çš„é¡ºåºæ‰“å°ï¼Œæ¯ä¸€å±‚æ‰“å°åˆ°ä¸€è¡Œã€‚

åŠ›æ‰£ï¼šç”¨ä¾‹æµ‹è¯•

æ€è·¯åˆ†æï¼š

å°†èŠ‚ç‚¹ä¿å­˜åˆ°å®¹å™¨ä¸­ã€‚æ¯ç»è¿‡ä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œå¼¹å‡ºå®¹å™¨ä¸­çš„è¯¥èŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œå¹¶å°†è¯¥èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å·¦å³å­èŠ‚ç‚¹ä¿å­˜åˆ°è¯¥å®¹å™¨å°¾å·´å¤„ã€‚éå†è¯¥å®¹å™¨ã€‚åŒæ—¶å®šä¹‰ä¸¤ä¸ªå˜é‡ï¼Œåˆ†åˆ«è®°å½•æœ¬å±‚èŠ‚ç‚¹æ•°ä»¥åŠä¸‹å±‚èŠ‚ç‚¹æ•°ã€‚

public List<List<Integer>> levelOrder(TreeNode root) {
    if(root == null){
        return new ArrayList();
    }
    Queue<TreeNode> queue = new LinkedList<>();
    queue.add(root);
    int now = 1;
    int next = 0;
    List<List<Integer>> list = new ArrayList<>();
    List<Integer> listTemp = new ArrayList<>();
    listTemp.add(root.val);
    list.add(listTemp);
    while(queue.size() != 0){
        listTemp = new ArrayList<>();
        while(now != 0){
            TreeNode node = queue.poll();
            now--;
            if(node.left != null){
                queue.add(node.left);
                listTemp.add(node.left.val);
                next++;
            }
            if(node.right != null){
                queue.add(node.right);
                listTemp.add(node.right.val);
                next++;
            }
        }
        if(next != 0){
            list.add(listTemp);
            now = next;
            next = 0;
        }
    }
    return list;
}

32.3 ä¹‹å­—å½¢æ‰“å°äºŒå‰æ ‘

é¢˜ç›®ï¼š

è¯·å®ç°ä¸€ä¸ªå‡½æ•°æŒ‰ç…§ä¹‹å­—å½¢é¡ºåºæ‰“å°äºŒå‰æ ‘ï¼Œå³ç¬¬ä¸€è¡ŒæŒ‰ç…§ä»å·¦åˆ°å³çš„é¡ºåºæ‰“å°ï¼Œç¬¬äºŒå±‚æŒ‰ç…§ä»å³åˆ°å·¦çš„é¡ºåºæ‰“å°ï¼Œç¬¬ä¸‰è¡Œå†æŒ‰ç…§ä»å·¦åˆ°å³çš„é¡ºåºæ‰“å°ï¼Œå…¶ä»–è¡Œä»¥æ­¤ç±»æ¨ã€‚

åŠ›æ‰£ï¼šç”¨ä¾‹æµ‹è¯•

æ€è·¯åˆ†æï¼š

  1. è¿™é‡Œæ¯ä¸€è¡Œéƒ½å¾—ä»å°¾éƒ¨å¼€å§‹å¯»æ‰¾å®ƒçš„å­—èŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œå› æ­¤å¯ç”¨æ ˆç»“æ„ã€‚
  2. å‚è€ƒé¢˜è§£ï¼Œä»£ç æ›´ç®€æ´ã€‚ç”¨ res ä¸­çš„å…ƒç´ ä¸ªæ•°èƒ½å¤Ÿåˆ¤æ–­å¤„åœ¨å¥‡æ•°è¡Œè¿˜æ˜¯å¶æ•°è¡Œï¼›ç”¨åŒç«¯é“¾è¡¨åŠ ä¸Šåè½¬æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œèƒ½å¤Ÿå¤§å¤§åŒ–ç®€æ“ä½œã€‚åœ¨ for å¾ªç¯ä¸­ï¼Œåˆå§‹åŒ– i çš„å€¼ä¸º sizeï¼Œè¿™æ ·è™½ç„¶åœ¨å¾ªç¯ä¸­ size ä¸æ–­åœ¨å˜åŒ–ï¼Œä½†æ˜¯è¿™ä¸ªå¾ªç¯æ¬¡æ•°è¿˜æ˜¯æ’å®šçš„ã€‚
public List<List<Integer>> levelOrder(TreeNode root) {
    if(root == null){
        return new ArrayList();
    }
    boolean flag = true;
    List<List<Integer>> res = new ArrayList<>();
    List<Integer> list = new ArrayList<>();
    list.add(root.val);
    res.add(list);
    Stack<TreeNode> stack = new Stack<>();
    stack.push(root);
    Stack<TreeNode> stackNext = null;
    int now = 1;
    int next = 0;
    while(stack.size() != 0){
        list = new ArrayList<>();
        stackNext = new Stack<>();
        while(now != 0){
            TreeNode node = stack.pop();
            now--;
            if(flag){
                if(node.right != null){
                    stackNext.push(node.right);
                    list.add(node.right.val);
                    next++;
                }
                if(node.left != null){
                    stackNext.push(node.left);
                    list.add(node.left.val);
                    next++;
                }
            }else{
                if(node.left != null){
                    stackNext.push(node.left);
                    list.add(node.left.val);
                    next++;
                }
                if(node.right != null){
                    stackNext.push(node.right);
                    list.add(node.right.val);
                    next++;
                }
            }
        }
        flag = !flag;
        if(next != 0){
            now = next;
            next = 0;
            res.add(list);
            stack = stackNext;
        }
    }
    return res;
}

å¤„ç†ä¸€ä¸ªäºŒå‰æ ‘çš„éå†åºåˆ—ï¼Œå¯ä»¥æ‰¾åˆ°äºŒå‰æ ‘çš„æ ¹èŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œå†åŸºäºæ ¹èŠ‚ç‚¹å°†åºåˆ—æ‹†åˆ†ä¸ºå·¦å­æ ‘å’Œå³å­æ ‘ã€‚

public boolean verifyPostorder(int[] postorder) {
    if(postorder == null){
        return false;
    }
    if(postorder.length <= 0){
        return true;
    }
    return verifyPostorderRecu(postorder, 0, postorder.length - 1);
}

private boolean verifyPostorderRecu(int[] postorder, int begin, int end){
    if(begin >= end){
        return true;
    }
    int temp = begin;
    if(postorder[temp] < postorder[end]){
        while(postorder[temp] < postorder[end]){
            temp++;
        }
        for(int i = temp; i < end; i++){
            if(postorder[i] < postorder[end]){
                return false;
            }
        }
        return verifyPostorderRecu(postorder, begin, temp - 1) && verifyPostorderRecu(postorder, temp, end - 1);
    }else{
        for(int i = temp; i < end; i++){
            if(postorder[i] < postorder[end]){
                return false;
            }
        }
        return verifyPostorderRecu(postorder, temp, end - 1);
    }
}

private List<List<Integer>> res = new ArrayList<>();

public List<List<Integer>> pathSum(TreeNode root, int sum) {
    if(root == null){
        return res;
    }
    pathSumRecu(root, sum, new ArrayList<Integer>());
    return res;
}

private void pathSumRecu(TreeNode node, int sum, List<Integer> temp){
    sum = sum - node.val;
    temp.add(node.val);
    if(node.left == null && node.right == null && sum == 0){
        res.add(new ArrayList<>(temp));
    }
    if(node.left != null){
        pathSumRecu(node.left, sum, temp);
    }
    if(node.right != null){
        pathSumRecu(node.right, sum, temp);
    }
    temp.remove(temp.size() - 1);
}

  1. å¯ç”¨ç©ºé—´æ¢æ—¶é—´ï¼Œåˆ©ç”¨ä¸€ä¸ª HashMapï¼Œkey ä¸ºåŸèŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œvalue ä¸ºå¤åˆ¶èŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œé€šè¿‡get(node).next = get(node.next)ä»¥åŠget(node).random = get(node.random)ï¼Œå¯å®ç°å¤åˆ¶ã€‚
  2. ä¸ç‰ºç‰²ç©ºé—´ï¼Œåˆ†ä¸‰æ­¥ã€‚1. å°†åŸé“¾è¡¨ A-B-C-D å˜ä¸º A-Aâ€˜-B-Bâ€™-C-Câ€™-D-Dâ€™ï¼Œå³å°†å¤åˆ¶èŠ‚ç‚¹æ’å…¥åœ¨åŸèŠ‚ç‚¹åé¢ã€‚2. é‚£ä¹ˆå¤åˆ¶èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„ random å³ä¸ºåŸèŠ‚ç‚¹çš„ random çš„ nextã€‚3. æ‹†åˆ†å‡ºåŸå§‹é“¾è¡¨å’Œå¤åˆ¶é“¾è¡¨ã€‚
  public Node copyRandomList(Node head) {
      if(head == null){
          return null;
      }
      
      // ç¬¬ä¸€æ­¥ åˆå¹¶
      Node temp =head;
      while(temp != null){
          Node tempNext = temp.next;
          temp.next = new Node(temp.val);
          temp.next.next = tempNext;
          temp = tempNext;
      }

      // ç¬¬äºŒæ­¥ å¤åˆ¶random
      temp = head;
      while(temp != null){
          if(temp.random != null){
              temp.next.random = temp.random.next;
          }else{
              temp.next.random = null;
          }
          temp = temp.next.next;
      }

// ç¬¬ä¸‰æ­¥ åˆ†ç¦»å‡ºåŸå§‹é“¾è¡¨å’Œå¤åˆ¶é“¾è¡¨
      temp = head;
      Node tempNew = head.next;
      while(temp != null && temp.next != null){
          Node tempTemp = temp.next;
          temp.next = temp.next.next;
          temp = tempTemp;
      }
      return tempNew;
  }

Node head;
Node pre;
public Node treeToDoublyList(Node root) {
    if(root == null){
        return root;
    }
    dfs(root);
    head.left = pre;
    pre.right = head;
    return head;
}

private void dfs(Node cur){
    if(cur == null) return;
    dfs(cur.left);
    if(pre == null){
        head = cur;
    }else{
        pre.right = cur;
        cur.left = pre;
    }
    pre = cur;
    dfs(cur.right);
}

// Encodes a tree to a single string.
public String serialize(TreeNode root) {
    if(root == null){
        return "";
    }
    return serializeRecu(root, "");
}

private String serializeRecu(TreeNode node, String s){
    if(node == null){
        return s + "None,";
    }else{
        s = s + node.val + ",";
        s = serializeRecu(node.left, s);
        s = serializeRecu(node.right, s);
    }
    return s;
}

// Decodes your encoded data to tree.
public TreeNode deserialize(String data) {
    if("".equals(data)){
        return null;
    }
    String[] dataArray = data.split(",");
    List<String> data_list = new LinkedList<String>(Arrays.asList(dataArray));
    return deserializeRecu(data_list);
}

private TreeNode deserializeRecu(List<String> list){
    if("None".equals(list.get(0))){
        list.remove(0);
        return null;
    }
    TreeNode temp = new TreeNode(Integer.valueOf(list.get(0)));
    list.remove(0);
    temp.left = deserializeRecu(list);
    temp.right = deserializeRecu(list);
    return temp;
}

char[] c;
List<String> list = new ArrayList<>();
public String[] permutation(String s) {
    if(s == null){
        return null;
    }
    c = s.toCharArray();
    dfs(0);
    return list.toArray(new String[list.size()]);
}

private void dfs(int index){
    if(index == c.length - 1){
        list.add(String.valueOf(c));
    }
    Set<Character> set = new HashSet<>();
    for(int i = index; i < c.length; i++){
        if(set.contains(c[i])){
            continue; // å‰ªæ
        }
        set.add(c[i]);
        swap(index, i);
        dfs(index + 1);
        swap(index, i);
    }
}

private void swap(int a, int b){
    char temp = c[a];
    c[a] = c[b];
    c[b] = temp;
}

public int majorityElement(int[] nums) {
    int target = 0;
    int count = 0;
    for(int num : nums){
        if(count == 0)  target = num;
        count += target == num ? 1 : -1;
    }
    return target;
}

public int[] getLeastNumbers(int[] arr, int k) {
    if(arr == null || k >= arr.length){
        return arr;
    }
    if(k <= 0){
        return new int[0];
    }
    int begin = 0;
    int end = arr.length - 1;
    int index;
    while(true){
        index = quickSortDemo(arr, begin, end);
        if(index == k - 1){
            return Arrays.copyOf(arr, k);
        }else if(index > k - 1){
            end = index - 1;
        }else{
            begin = index + 1;
        }
    }
}

private int quickSortDemo(int[] arr, int begin, int end){
    int beginSave = begin;
    int temp = arr[begin];
    while(end > begin){
        while(end > begin && arr[end] > temp)   end--;
        while(end > begin && arr[begin] <= temp)   begin++;
        if(end != begin){
            int temp2 = arr[begin];
            arr[begin] = arr[end];
            arr[end] = temp2;
        }
    }
    arr[beginSave] = arr[begin];
    arr[begin] = temp;
    return begin;
}

  2. find æ•°æ®æ—¶ï¼Œè‹¥ä¸¤ä¸ªå †ä¸­æ•°æ®ä¸ªæ•°ä¸ç›¸åŒï¼Œåˆ™ä¸­ä½æ•°ä¸ºæœ€å¤§å †çš„æ ¹èŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼›è‹¥ä¸¤ä¸ªå †ä¸­æ•°æ®ä¸ªæ•°ç›¸åŒï¼Œåˆ™ä¸­ä½æ•°ä¸ºä¸¤ä¸ªå †ä¸­æ ¹èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å¹³å‡æ•°ã€‚
Queue<Integer> large,small;
/** initialize your data structure here. */
public MedianFinder() {
    large = new PriorityQueue<>( (x, y) -> (y - x) );
    small = new PriorityQueue<>();
}

public void addNum(int num) {
    if(large.size() != small.size()){
        large.offer(num);
        small.offer(large.poll());
    }else{
        small.offer(num);
        large.offer(small.poll());
    }
}

public double findMedian() {
    return large.size() == small.size() ? (double)(large.peek() + small.peek()) / (double)2.0 
                                        : large.peek();
}

é‡‡ç”¨åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’æ³•ã€‚è®¾ä»¥ç´¢å¼•ä¸º i çš„å…ƒç´ ç»“å°¾çš„å­æ•°ç»„çš„æœ€å¤§å’Œä¸º dp[i]ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆå½“ dp[i - 1] <= 0 æ—¶ï¼Œdp[i] = data[i]ï¼›å½“ dp[i - 1] > 0 æ—¶ï¼Œdp[i] = dp[i - 1] + data[i]ã€‚æœ€åæ‰€éœ€ç»“æœå°±æ˜¯ dp ä¸­çš„æœ€å¤§å€¼ï¼Œè€Œè¿™é‡Œç”±äºåŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’æ—¶ï¼Œåªéœ€è¦ä¸Šä¸€è½®çš„ dp æ¥å¾—åˆ°è¿™ä¸€è½®çš„ dpï¼Œå› æ­¤ dp ä¸éœ€è¦æ•°ç»„æ¥å­˜æ”¾ï¼Œç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ä¸ºO(1)ã€‚

public int maxSubArray(int[] nums) {
    if(nums == null || nums.length <= 0){
        throw new RuntimeException("è¾“å…¥æ•°æ®ä¸åˆæ³•ï¼");
    }
    int res = nums[0];
    int dp = res;
    for(int i = 1; i < nums.length; i++){
        dp = dp <= 0 ? nums[i] : dp + nums[i];
        res = dp <= res ? res : dp;
    }
    return res;
}

  2. è®¾æ•°å­—æ˜¯ x ä½æ•°ï¼Œè®°ç¬¬ i ä½ä¸º n(i)ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆè¾“å…¥çš„æ•°å­—ä¸º n(x) n(x-1) n(x-2) â€¦ n1ã€‚
  3. ç§° n(i) ä¸ºå½“å‰ä½ï¼Œè®°ä¸º curï¼›

public int countDigitOne(int n) {
    if(n <= 0){
        return 0;
    }
    int cur = n % 10;
    int high = n / 10;
    int low = 0;
    int digit = 1;
    int res = 0;
    while(high != 0 || cur !=0){
        if(cur == 0)        res += (high * digit);
        else if(cur == 1)   res +=  (high * digit + low + 1);
        else                res += ((high + 1) * digit);
        low += (cur * digit);
        cur = high % 10;
        high /= 10;
        digit *= 10;
    }
    return res;
}

  5. ç¬¬ä¸€æ­¥ï¼Œç¡®å®šè¯¥æ•°ä½æ‰€å±çš„æ•°å­—ä¸ºå‡ ä½æ•°ï¼›ç¬¬äºŒæ­¥ï¼Œç¡®å®šå‡ºè¯¥æ•°å­—ï¼›ç¬¬ä¸‰æ­¥ï¼Œç¡®å®šå‡ºè¯¥æ•°ä½ã€‚
public int findNthDigit(int n) {
    if(n < 0){
        throw new RuntimeException("è¾“å…¥æ•°æ®å¼‚å¸¸ï¼");
    }
    long start = 1;
    int digit = 1;
    long count = 9;
    while(n > count){
        n -= count;
        start *= 10;
        digit++;
        count = start * digit * 9;
    }
    long num = start + (n - 1) / digit;
    return Integer.valueOf(String.valueOf(num).charAt((n - 1) % digit) - '0');  //æ³¨æ„ï¼Œå­—ç¬¦è¿™é‡Œä¼šè½¬æ¢ä¸ºASCIIç ï¼Œå› æ­¤è¦ å‡'0'
}

  1. å®šä¹‰ä¸€ä¸ªæ’åºè§„åˆ™ï¼šè®¾ä¸¤ä¸ªä»¥å­—ç¬¦ä¸²å½¢å¼è¡¨ç¤ºçš„æ•°å­—åˆ†åˆ«ä¸º x å’Œ yï¼Œè¿™é‡Œçš„åŠ å·è¡¨ç¤ºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ‹¼æ¥ï¼Œå°†ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°å­—æ‹¼æ¥åœ¨ä¸€èµ·ã€‚è‹¥ x + y > y + xï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆ x > yï¼›è‹¥ x + y < y + xï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆ x < yã€‚è¿™æ ·çš„æ’åºè§„åˆ™éœ€è¦æ»¡è¶³ä¸‰ä¸ªæ¡ä»¶ï¼šè‡ªåæ€§ã€å¯¹ç§°æ€§å’Œä¼ é€’æ€§ã€‚è¿™ä¸‰ä¸ªè¯æ˜ç•¥ã€‚
  2. å°†æ•°å­—æ•°ç»„è½¬ä¸ºå¯¹åº”çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ•°ç»„ï¼Œç„¶åå¯¹å­—ç¬¦ä¸²æ•°ç»„æŒ‰ç…§ä¸Šè¿°çš„æ’åºè§„åˆ™ä»å°åˆ°å¤§è¿›è¡Œæ’åºï¼ˆè¿™é‡Œæ¼”ç¤ºçš„æ˜¯å¿«æ’ï¼‰ã€‚å°†æ’åºå¥½çš„æ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä»å·¦åˆ°å³æ‹¼æ¥èµ·æ¥å³å¯å¾—åˆ°ç­”æ¡ˆã€‚
public String minNumber(int[] nums) {
    if(nums == null){
        throw new RuntimeException("è¾“å…¥æ•°æ®ä¸åˆæ³•ï¼");
    }
    String[] strs = new String[nums.length];
    for(int i = 0; i < nums.length; i++){
        strs[i] = String.valueOf(nums[i]);
    }
    quickSort(strs, 0, nums.length - 1);
    StringBuilder res = new StringBuilder();
    for(String s : strs){
        res.append(s);
    }
    return res.toString();
}

private void quickSort(String[] strs, int begin, int end){
    if(begin >= end){
        return;
    }
    int i = begin;
    int j = end;
    String tempVal = strs[begin];
    while(i < j){
        while(j > i && (strs[j] + tempVal).compareTo(tempVal + strs[j]) > 0){
            j--;
        }
        while(j > i && (strs[i] + tempVal).compareTo(tempVal + strs[i]) <=0){
            i++;
        }
        if(j != i){
            String temp = strs[i];
            strs[i] = strs[j];
            strs[j] = temp;
        }
    }
    strs[begin] = strs[i];
    strs[i] = tempVal;
    quickSort(strs, begin, i - 1);
    quickSort(strs, i + 1, end);
}

åŠ›æ‰£ï¼šç”¨ä¾‹æµ‹è¯•

æ€è·¯åˆ†æï¼š

åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’æ³•ã€‚dp[i] è¡¨ç¤ºä»¥ç¬¬ i ä¸ªæ•°å­—ç»“å°¾çš„å­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„ç¿»è¯‘æ–¹æ³•ç§æ•°ã€‚è¿™é‡Œç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°å­—ä¸æ˜¯ i = 0 è€Œæ˜¯ i = 1ã€‚ä»å·¦å¾€å³å’Œä»å³å¾€å·¦æ˜¯ä¸€æ ·çš„ã€‚è¿™é‡Œç”¨ä»å·¦å¾€å³è¿›è¡Œè®²è§£ï¼Œä½†ä»£ç é‡‡ç”¨ä»å³å¾€å·¦çš„æ–¹å¼ï¼Œä»¥å®ç°ä½ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦çš„æ–¹æ³•ã€‚

  1. å½“å‰æ•°å­—å’Œå‰ä¸€ä½æ•°å­—ç»„æˆçš„æ•°ï¼Œè‹¥åœ¨ 10~25 ä¹‹é—´ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆä»¥å½“å‰æ•°å­—ç»“å°¾çš„æ•°å­—ï¼Œæœ‰ dp[i-1] + dp[i-2] ç§ç¿»è¯‘æ–¹å¼ï¼›è‹¥ä¸åœ¨é‚£ä¸ªåŒºé—´å†…ï¼Œåˆ™æœ‰ dp[i-1] ç§ç¿»è¯‘æ–¹å¼ã€‚
  2. æ³¨æ„åˆ° dp åªç”¨å­˜ä¸¤ä½çš„æ•°æ®ï¼Œå› æ­¤ dp åªç”¨ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•´æ•°å˜é‡å­˜æ”¾å³å¯ï¼Œé™ä½ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ã€‚åˆå§‹åŒ– dp[0] = dp[1] = 1ã€‚
  3. æ¥ä¸‹æ¥å°±æ˜¯å¦‚ä½•éå†æ•°å­—ï¼Œç¬¬ä¸€ç§æ–¹å¼æ˜¯ï¼Œè½¬ä¸ºå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œé¡ºåºéå†ï¼Œè¿™æ ·éœ€è¦O(n)çš„ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ä»¥å­˜æ”¾å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ã€‚ç¬¬äºŒç§æ–¹å¼æ˜¯åˆ©ç”¨æ•°å­—çš„æ±‚ä½™æ±‚æ¨¡è¿ç®—ï¼Œä»å³å¾€å·¦éå†æ•°å­—ã€‚
public int translateNum(int num) {
    int dpNew = 1;
    int dpOld = 1;
    int tempA = num % 10;
    int tempB = -1;
    while(num != 0){
        num /= 10;
        tempB = num % 10;
        int temp = tempB * 10 + tempA;
        int c = (temp >= 10 && temp <= 25) ? dpNew + dpOld : dpNew;
        dpOld = dpNew;
        dpNew = c;
        tempA = tempB;
    }
    return dpNew;
}

åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’æ³•ã€‚dp[i] [j] è¡¨ç¤ºåˆ°è¾¾è¡Œç´¢å¼•ä¸º iã€åˆ—ç´¢å¼•ä¸º jçš„æ ¼å­èƒ½æ‹¿åˆ°ç¤¼ç‰©çš„æœ€å¤§ä»·å€¼ã€‚æ˜¾ç„¶ï¼Œä¸€èˆ¬æƒ…å†µä¸‹ï¼š

dp[i][j]=max(dp[iâˆ’1][j],dp[i][jâˆ’1])+grid[i][j]dp[i][j] = max(dp[i-1][j],dp[i][j-1]) + grid[i][j]dp[i][j]=max(dp[iâˆ’1][j],dp[i][jâˆ’1])+grid[i][j]

ä¸ºé™ä½ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼Œå¯å°† dp ç›´æ¥å»ºç«‹åœ¨è¾“å…¥æ•°ç»„ä¸­ã€‚ç¬¬ 0 è¡Œå’Œç¬¬ 0 åˆ—ä¸ºç‰¹æ®Šæƒ…å†µï¼Œéœ€è¦åˆ¤æ–­ï¼Œä¸ºäº†ä¸åœ¨å¾ªç¯ä¸­è¿›è¡Œå¤§é‡çš„åˆ¤æ–­ï¼Œå¯åœ¨åˆå§‹åŒ–æ—¶å…ˆå¯¹ç¬¬ 0 è¡Œå’Œç¬¬ 0 åˆ—è¿›è¡Œå¤„ç†ã€‚

è‹¥ä¸æƒ³æ”¹å˜åŸæ•°ç»„ï¼Œä¹Ÿä¸å¿…å»ºç«‹ M x N çš„ dp çŸ©é˜µã€‚æ³¨æ„åˆ°æˆ‘ä»¬ä¸éœ€è¦å½“å‰è¡Œçš„å‰ä¸¤è¡ŒåŠä¹‹å‰çš„æ•°æ®ï¼Œå› æ­¤åªéœ€è¦å»ºç«‹ä¸€ä¸ªä¸€ç»´æ•°ç»„ï¼Œé•¿åº¦ä¸º N ã€‚ä¸æ–­æ›´æ–°è¯¥æ•°ç»„å³å¯ã€‚

public int maxValue(int[][] grid) {
    if(grid == null || grid.length <= 0 || grid[0].length <= 0){
        throw new RuntimeException("è¾“å…¥æ•°æ®å¼‚å¸¸ï¼");
    }
    for(int i = 1; i < grid.length; i++){
        grid[i][0] += grid[i-1][0];
    }
    for(int j = 1; j < grid[0].length; j++){
        grid[0][j] += grid[0][j-1];
    }
    for(int i = 1; i <grid.length; i++){
        for(int j = 1; j < grid[0].length; j++){
            grid[i][j] += Math.max(grid[i-1][j], grid[i][j-1]);
        }
    }
    return grid[grid.length - 1][grid[0].length - 1];
}

  2. è‹¥ç´¢å¼•ä¸º i çš„å…ƒç´ ä¸ä¹‹å‰çš„å…ƒç´ æ²¡æœ‰é‡å¤ï¼Œåˆ™ dp[i] = dp[i-1] + 1;è‹¥æœ‰é‡å¤ï¼Œåˆ™è¿›ä¸€æ­¥åˆ¤æ–­ï¼›
  3. é‡å¤åï¼Œåˆ¤æ–­ä¸Šä¸€æ¬¡é‡å¤çš„å…ƒç´ æ˜¯å¦åœ¨å½“å‰å¾—åˆ°çš„æœ€å¤§å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¹‹å‰ï¼Œä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯å½“å‰å…ƒç´ ä¸å®ƒçš„æœ€è¿‘é‡å¤çš„é‚£ä¸ªå…ƒç´ çš„è·ç¦» d æ˜¯å¦å¤§äº dp[i-1]ï¼Œè‹¥å¤§äºï¼Œåˆ™è¯¥é‡å¤å…ƒç´ ä¸å¯¹æœ¬æ¬¡è§„åˆ’é€ æˆå½±å“ï¼Œå®ƒåœ¨è¯¥å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„å‰é¢ï¼Œåˆ™ dp[i] = dp[i-1] + 1ï¼›è‹¥ä¸å¤§äºï¼Œåˆ™è¯¥é‡å¤å…ƒç´ å°±åœ¨è¯¥å­å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¹‹ä¸­ï¼Œdp[i] = dã€‚
  4. é‡‡ç”¨ä¸€ä¸ªHashMapè®°å½•æ¯ä¸ªå…ƒç´ æœ€æ–°çš„ç´¢å¼•ï¼Œç”±äºæ˜¯å­—ç¬¦ï¼ŒHashMapé”®å€¼å¯¹æ•°é‡æœ‰ä¸Šé™ï¼Œå› æ­¤ç©ºé—´å¤æ‚åº¦ä¸ºO(1)ï¼Œæ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ä¸ºO(1)ã€‚å› æ­¤å¯ä»¥ç”¨é•¿åº¦å›ºå®šçš„æ•°ç»„å¸¦æ›¿ï¼Œæ•°ç»„æ“ä½œæ¯”hashmapå¿«ã€‚
public int lengthOfLongestSubstring(String s) {
    if(s == null || s.length() == 0)   return 0;
    HashMap<Character,Integer> hashmap = new HashMap<>();
    int dp = 1;
    int res = dp;
    hashmap.put(s.charAt(0), 0);
    for(int i = 1; i < s.length(); i++){
        char temp = s.charAt(i);
        if(hashmap.get(temp) == null){
            dp++;
        }else{
            if(i - hashmap.get(temp) > dp){
                dp++;
            }else{
                dp = i - hashmap.get(temp);
            }
        }
        res = dp > res? dp : res;
        hashmap.put(temp, i);
    }
    return res;
}

æˆ‘ä»¬æŠŠåªåŒ…å«è´¨å› å­ 2ã€3 å’Œ 5 çš„æ•°ç§°ä½œä¸‘æ•°ï¼ˆUgly Numberï¼‰ã€‚æ±‚æŒ‰ä»å°åˆ°å¤§çš„é¡ºåºçš„ç¬¬ n ä¸ªä¸‘æ•°ã€‚

åŠ›æ‰£ï¼šç”¨ä¾‹æµ‹è¯•

åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’ã€‚

  3. é‡‡å–ç”¨ä¸‰ä¸ªæŒ‡é’ˆçš„æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œp2,p3,p5
  4. p2æŒ‡å‘çš„æ•°å­—ä¸‹ä¸€æ¬¡ä¹˜ä¸Š2ï¼Œp3æŒ‡å‘çš„æ•°å­—ä¸‹ä¸€æ¬¡ä¹˜ä¸Š3ï¼Œp5æŒ‡å‘çš„æ•°å­—ä¹˜ä¸Š5
  5. æˆ‘ä»¬ä» 2p2 3p3 5p5 é€‰å–æœ€å°çš„ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°å­—ï¼Œä½œä¸ºç¬¬kä¸ªä¸‘æ•°
  6. å¦‚æœ ç¬¬Kä¸ªä¸‘æ•° == 2p2ï¼Œä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯è¯´å‰é¢0-p2ä¸ªä¸‘æ•°*2ä¸å¯èƒ½äº§ç”Ÿæ¯”ç¬¬Kä¸ªä¸‘æ•°æ›´å¤§çš„ä¸‘æ•°äº†ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥p2++
  7. p3,p5åŒç†
  8. è¿”å›ç¬¬nä¸ªä¸‘æ•°
  9. ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªä¸‘æ•°æ˜¯ 1ï¼Œä»¥ 1 åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸‘æ•°è¡¨ã€‚æ³¨æ„ç¬¬6ã€7æ­¥éœ€è¦ç”¨ if è€Œä¸èƒ½æ˜¯ if elseï¼Œå› ä¸ºæŸäº›ä¸‘æ•°èƒ½æœ‰å¤šç§æƒ…å†µè¢«å¾—åˆ°ï¼Œ
public int nthUglyNumber(int n) {
    if(n <= 0){
        throw new RuntimeException("è¾“å…¥æ•°æ®å¼‚å¸¸ï¼");
    }
    int[] dp = new int[n];
    dp[0] = 1;
    int p2 = 0;
    int p3 = 0;
    int p5 = 0;
    for(int i = 1; i < n; i++){
        dp[i] = Math.min(dp[p2] * 2, Math.min(dp[p3] * 3, dp[p5] * 5));
        if(dp[p2] * 2 == dp[i]) p2++;
        if(dp[p3] * 3 == dp[i]) p3++;
        if(dp[p5] * 5 == dp[i]) p5++;
    }
    return dp[n - 1];
}

è‹¥æ²¡é™„åŠ  s åªåŒ…å«å°å†™å­—æ¯ï¼Œåˆ™å¯èƒ½æœ‰ä¸­æ–‡å­—ç¬¦ç­‰ã€‚è¿™æ˜¯å¯ä»¥ç”¨HashMapæ¥å­˜æ”¾ä¿¡æ¯ã€‚è¿›ä¸€æ­¥çš„ï¼Œå¯ä»¥é‡‡ç”¨æœ‰åºå“ˆå¸Œè¡¨ LinkedHashMapï¼Œç¬¬äºŒè½®éå†æ—¶ä¸éœ€è¦éå†åŸå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œè¿™æ ·ä¼šæœ‰å¤§é‡é‡å¤å­—ç¬¦çš„éå†ï¼Œè€Œåªç”¨éå†æœ‰åºå“ˆå¸Œè¡¨ï¼Œå› ä¸ºæœ‰åºå“ˆå¸Œè¡¨æ˜¯æŒ‰æ’å…¥é¡ºåºæ’åºçš„ã€‚

  1. è¾“å…¥ä¸¤ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œä»ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­åˆ é™¤åœ¨ç¬¬äºŒä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­å‡ºç°è¿‡çš„æ‰€æœ‰å­—ç¬¦ã€‚ç”¨æ•°ç»„å½“ä½œå“ˆå¸Œè¡¨ï¼Œå°†ç¬¬äºŒä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²çš„å­—ç¬¦å‡ºç°ä¿¡æ¯å­˜å…¥æ•°ç»„ä¸­ã€‚å†éå†ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ï¼Œæ¯æ¬¡åˆ¤æ–­è¯¥å­—ç¬¦æ˜¯å¦å‡ºç°å†ç¬¬äºŒä¸ªå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­ï¼Œæ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦ä¸ºO(1) * O(N)ã€‚

  2. åˆ é™¤å­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­é‡å¤å‡ºç°çš„å­—ç¬¦ã€‚å¦‚ â€œgoogleâ€ è¢«åˆ é™¤ä¸º â€œgoleâ€ã€‚è¿™ä¹Ÿå¯ä»¥ç”¨ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ç»„å­˜æ”¾å­—ç¬¦æ˜¯å¦å‡ºç°è¿‡çš„ä¿¡æ¯ã€‚

æ€»çš„æ¥è¯´ï¼Œåœ¨ä¸€äº›æƒ…å†µä¸‹ï¼Œå¯ä»¥ç”¨æ•°ç»„ä»£æ›¿å“ˆå¸Œè¡¨ï¼Œæé«˜æ—¶é—´æ•ˆç‡ã€‚

public char firstUniqChar(String s) {
    int[] num = new int[128];
    for(int i = 0; i < s.length(); i++){
        num[s.charAt(i)]++;
    }
    for(int i = 0; i < s.length(); i++){
        char temp = s.charAt(i);
        if(num[temp] == 1){
            return temp;
        }
    }
    return ' ';
}

ç”¨ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ï¼Œå…ƒç´ åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸º -1ï¼Œç´¢å¼•ä¸ºå­—ç¬¦çš„ASCIIç ï¼Œæ¯å½“åŠ å…¥ä¸€ä¸ªå­—ç¬¦æ—¶ï¼Œåˆ¤æ–­è¯¥å­—ç¬¦ä½ç½®å¯¹åº”çš„å…ƒç´ æ˜¯å¦ä¸º -1ï¼Œè‹¥æ˜¯ï¼Œåˆ™å°†è¯¥å­—ç¬¦å‡ºç°çš„ç´¢å¼•æ”¾å…¥è¯¥æ•°ç»„å¯¹åº”ä½ç½®ä¸­ï¼›è‹¥å¤§äºç­‰äº 0ï¼Œåˆ™å·²å‡ºç°è¿‡ï¼Œå°†æ•°ç»„ä¸­è¯¥ä½ç½®å…ƒç´ ç½®ä¸º -2ï¼Œåˆ™ä¸éœ€è¦æ“ä½œã€‚

public int reversePairs(int[] nums) {
    if(nums == null || nums.length <= 1){
        return 0;
    }
    int length = nums.length;
    int[] copy = new int[length]; //ä¸ä¿®æ”¹åŸæ•°ç»„
    for(int i = 0; i < length; i++){
        copy[i] = nums[i];
    }
    int[] temp = new int[length];
    return mergeSort(copy, 0, length - 1, temp);
}

private int mergeSort(int[] nums, int begin, int end, int[] temp){
    if(begin == end){
        return 0;
    }
    int mid = begin + (end - begin) / 2; //é¿å…å‡ºç°äºŒåˆ†æ³•ç»å…¸æº¢å‡ºbug
    int count1 = mergeSort(nums, begin, mid, temp);
    int count2 = mergeSort(nums, mid + 1, end, temp);
    int count3 = merge(nums, begin, mid, end, temp);
    return count1 + count2 + count3;
}

private int merge(int[] nums, int begin, int mid, int end, int[] temp){
    for(int i = begin; i <= end; i++){
        temp[i] = nums[i];
    }
    int i = begin;
    int j = mid + 1;
    int count = 0;
    for(int k = begin; k <= end; k++){
        if(i == mid + 1)    nums[k] = temp[j++];
        else if(j == end + 1)   nums[k] = temp[i++];
        else if(temp[i] <= temp[j])   nums[k] = temp[i++];
        else{
            nums[k] = temp[j++];
            count += (mid - i + 1); 
        }
    }
    return count;
}

   // æ–¹æ³•2
public ListNode getIntersectionNode(ListNode headA, ListNode headB) {
           int countA = 0;
           int countB = 0;
           ListNode tempA = headA;
           ListNode tempB = headB;
           while(tempA != null){
               tempA = tempA.next;
               countA++;
           }
           while(tempB != null){
               tempB = tempB.next;
               countB++;
           }
           while(countA > countB){
               headA = headA.next;
               countA--;
           }
           while(countA < countB){
               headB = headB.next;
               countB--;
           }
           while(headA != headB){
               headA = headA.next;
               headB = headB.next;
           }
           return headA;
     }

// æ–¹æ³•3
   public ListNode getIntersectionNode(ListNode headA, ListNode headB) {
       ListNode tempA = headA;
       ListNode tempB = headB;
       while(tempA != tempB){
           tempA = tempA == null ? headB : tempA.next;
           tempB = tempB == null ? headA : tempB.next;
       }
       return tempA;
   }

53.1ã€æ•°å­—åœ¨æ’åºæ•°ç»„ä¸­å‡ºç°çš„æ¬¡æ•°

ç»Ÿè®¡ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°å­—åœ¨æ’åºæ•°ç»„ä¸­å‡ºç°çš„æ¬¡æ•°ã€‚

åˆ©ç”¨äºŒåˆ†æ³•ï¼Œå¯»æ‰¾ target + 0.5 å’Œ target - 0.5 çš„ä½ç½®ï¼Œä¹Ÿå°±æ˜¯æƒ³æ‰¾åˆ° taget çš„å·¦å³è¾¹ç•Œã€‚

public int search(int[] nums, int target) {
    if(nums == null || nums.length <= 0){
        return 0;
    }
    int i = find(nums, 0, nums.length - 1, target + 0.5);
    if(i > 0 && nums[i - 1] != target)  return 0;
    int j = find(nums, 0, i - 1, target - 0.5);
    return i - j;
}

private int find(int[] nums, int begin, int end, double target){
    int i = begin;
    int j = end;
    while(i <= j){
        int mid = i + (j - i) / 2;
        if(nums[mid] < target)  i = mid + 1;
        else if(nums[mid] > target)    j = mid - 1;
    }
    return i;
}

ä¸€ä¸ªé•¿åº¦ä¸ºn-1çš„é€’å¢æ’åºæ•°ç»„ä¸­çš„æ‰€æœ‰æ•°å­—éƒ½æ˜¯å”¯ä¸€çš„ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”æ¯ä¸ªæ•°å­—éƒ½åœ¨èŒƒå›´0ï½n-1ä¹‹å†…ã€‚åœ¨èŒƒå›´0ï½n-1å†…çš„nä¸ªæ•°å­—ä¸­æœ‰ä¸”åªæœ‰ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°å­—ä¸åœ¨è¯¥æ•°ç»„ä¸­ï¼Œè¯·æ‰¾å‡ºè¿™ä¸ªæ•°å­—ã€‚

åˆ©ç”¨äºŒåˆ†æ³•ã€‚å·¦å­æ•°ç»„ä¸€å®šæ²¡æœ‰ç¼ºå¤±ï¼Œå³å­æ•°ç»„ä¸­åŒ…å«ç¼ºå¤±çš„æ•°å­—ã€‚é‚£ä¹ˆï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬éœ€è¦æ‰¾åˆ°å³å­æ•°ç»„çš„èµ·ç‚¹ã€‚è‹¥ nums[mid] != midï¼Œåˆ™è¯´æ˜æœ‰ç¼ºå¤±ï¼Œåˆ™ j = mid - 1ã€‚åä¹‹ï¼Œä¹Ÿå¯åˆ†æã€‚

public int missingNumber(int[] nums) {
    if(nums == null || nums.length <= 0){
        throw new RuntimeException("è¾“å…¥æ•°æ®å¼‚å¸¸");
    }
    int i = 0;
    int j = nums.length - 1;
    while(i <= j){
        int mid = i + (j - i) / 2;
        if(nums[mid] != mid)    j = mid - 1;
        else    i = mid + 1;
    }
    return i;
}

private int num = 0;
private int res = 0;
public int kthLargest(TreeNode root, int k) {
    if(root == null || k <= 0){
        throw new RuntimeException("è¾“å…¥æ•°æ®ä¸åˆæ³•ï¼");
    }
    num = k;
    midOrder(root);
    return res;
}

private void midOrder(TreeNode node){
    if(node.right != null){
        midOrder(node.right);
    }
    if(num == 0){
        return;
    }
    num--;
    if(num == 0){
        res = node.val;
    }
    if(node.left != null){
        midOrder(node.left);
    }
}

// æ–¹æ³•1
   public int maxDepth(TreeNode root) {
       if(root == null)    return 0;
       return Math.max(maxDepth(root.left), maxDepth(root.right)) + 1;
   }

// æ–¹æ³•2
   public int maxDepth(TreeNode root) {
       if(root == null)    return 0;
       Queue<TreeNode> queue = new LinkedList<>();
       queue.add(root);
       int res = 0;
       while(queue.size() != 0){
           res++;
           for(int i = queue.size(); i > 0; i--){
               TreeNode temp = queue.poll();
               if(temp.left != null)   queue.add(temp.left);
               if(temp.right != null)  queue.add(temp.right);
           }
       }
       return res;
   }

55.2 å¹³è¡¡äºŒå‰æ ‘

é¢˜ç›®ï¼š

æ²¿ç”¨ä¸Šä¸€é¢˜çš„æ€æƒ³ï¼Œè‹¥ä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å·¦å­æ ‘å³å­æ ‘æ·±åº¦ä¹‹å·®å¤§äº 1ï¼Œåˆ™ä¸æ˜¯å¹³è¡¡æ ‘ï¼Œè¿™é‡Œç”¨ -1 è¡¨ç¤ºã€‚

public boolean isBalanced(TreeNode root) {
    return recur(root) == -1 ? false : true;
}

private int recur(TreeNode node){
    if(node == null)    return 0;
    int left = recur(node.left);
    if(left == -1)  return -1;
    int right = recur(node.right);
    if(right == -1) return -1;
    return Math.abs(right - left) > 1 ? -1 : Math.max(right,left) + 1;
}

public int[] singleNumbers(int[] nums) {
    int res = xor(nums);
    int help = 1;
    while((res & 1) != 1){
        res = res >> 1;
        help = help << 1;
    }
    int a = 0;
    int b = 0;
    for(int num : nums){
        if((num & help) == 0)  a ^= num;
        else    b ^= num;
    }
    int[] target = {a,b};
    return target;
}

// å¯¹ä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ä¸­æ‰€æœ‰å…ƒç´ è¿›è¡Œå¼‚æˆ–
private int xor(int[] nums){
    int res = nums[0];  
    for(int i = 1; i < nums.length; i++){
        res ^= nums[i];
    }
    return res;
}

  2. æœ‰é™çŠ¶æ€æœºï¼šå› ä¸ºè¦è¢« 3 æ•´é™¤ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆ 1 å‡ºç°çš„æ¬¡æ•°ä¸º 0â€”>1---->2----->0â€¦ï¼ŒçŠ¶æ€æœ‰ 3 ä¸ªï¼Œå› æ­¤å¾—ç”¨ä¸¤ä½çš„ 0 å’Œ 1è¡¨ç¤ºï¼Œones è¡¨ç¤ºä½ä½ï¼Œtwos è¡¨ç¤ºé«˜ä½ã€‚åˆ—å‡ºçŠ¶æ€è½¬æ¢è¡¨ã€‚å¯æ€»ç»“å‡ºè§„å¾‹ã€‚
public int singleNumber(int[] nums) {
    int ones = 0;
    int twos = 0;
    for(int num : nums){
        ones = ones ^ num & ~twos;
        twos = twos ^ num & ~ones;
    }
    return ones;
}

57.1 å’Œä¸º s çš„ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°å­—

é¢˜ç›®ï¼š

è¾“å…¥ä¸€ä¸ªé€’å¢æ’åºçš„æ•°ç»„å’Œä¸€ä¸ªæ•°å­—sï¼Œåœ¨æ•°ç»„ä¸­æŸ¥æ‰¾ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°ï¼Œä½¿å¾—å®ƒä»¬çš„å’Œæ­£å¥½æ˜¯sã€‚å¦‚æœæœ‰å¤šå¯¹æ•°å­—çš„å’Œç­‰äºsï¼Œåˆ™è¾“å‡ºä»»æ„ä¸€å¯¹å³å¯ã€‚

å¯¹æ’åŒæŒ‡é’ˆã€‚åˆå§‹åŒ– begin = 0 ä»¥åŠ end = length - 1ï¼Œè‹¥è¿™ä¸¤ä¸ªæŒ‡é’ˆä¸Šå¯¹åº”å…ƒç´ ç›¸åŠ å°äºç›®æ ‡å…ƒç´ ï¼Œåˆ™ begin++ï¼›è‹¥å¤§äºï¼Œåˆ™ endâ€“ã€‚

public int[] twoSum(int[] nums, int target) {
    if(nums == null || nums.length == 0){
        throw new RuntimeException("è¾“å…¥æ•°æ®ä¸åˆæ³•ï¼");
    }
    int begin = 0;
    int end = nums.length - 1;
    while(begin < end && (nums[begin] + nums[end] != target)){
        while(begin < end && (nums[begin] + nums[end] < target)){
            begin++;
        }
        while(begin < end && (nums[begin] + nums[end] > target)){
            end--;
        }
    }
    int[] res = {nums[begin], nums[end]};
    return res;
}

57.2 å’Œä¸º s çš„è¿ç»­æ­£æ•°åºåˆ—

è¾“å…¥ä¸€ä¸ªæ­£æ•´æ•° target ï¼Œè¾“å‡ºæ‰€æœ‰å’Œä¸º target çš„è¿ç»­æ­£æ•´æ•°åºåˆ—ï¼ˆè‡³å°‘å«æœ‰ä¸¤ä¸ªæ•°ï¼‰ã€‚

åºåˆ—å†…çš„æ•°å­—ç”±å°åˆ°å¤§æ’åˆ—ï¼Œä¸åŒåºåˆ—æŒ‰ç…§é¦–ä¸ªæ•°å­—ä»å°åˆ°å¤§æ’åˆ—ã€‚

åŠ›æ‰£ï¼šç”¨ä¾‹æµ‹è¯•

æ€è·¯åˆ†æï¼š

ç±»ä¼¼ä¸Šé¢˜ï¼ŒåŒæŒ‡é’ˆï¼Œæ»‘åŠ¨çª—å£ã€‚è®¾å®šä¸€ä¸ªçª—å£ï¼Œè‹¥çª—å£å†…æ•°å­—å’Œå°äºç›®æ ‡æ•°å­—ï¼Œåˆ™çª—å£å³è¾¹ç•Œå‘å³æ‰©å¼ ï¼›è‹¥çª—å£å†…æ•°å­—å’Œå¤§äºç›®æ ‡æ•°å­—ï¼Œåˆ™çª—å£å·¦è¾¹ç•Œå‘å³ç¼©å°ï¼›è‹¥ç­‰äºï¼Œåˆ™ä¿å­˜ç»“æœï¼Œå°†çª—å£æ•´ä½“å‘å³å¹³ç§»ä¸€æ ¼ï¼Œè¿›è¡Œä¸‹ä¸ªè§£çš„å¯»æ‰¾ã€‚

public int[][] findContinuousSequence(int target) {
    if(target <= 2){
        throw new RuntimeException("è¾“å…¥æ•°æ®ä¸åˆæ³•ï¼");
    }
    int begin = 1;
    int end = 2;
    List<int[]> list = new ArrayList<>();
    while(begin <= target / 2){
        while(((begin + end) * (end - begin + 1)) / 2 < target){
            end++;
        }
        while(begin <= target / 2 && ((begin + end) * (end - begin + 1)) / 2 > target){
            begin++;
        }
        if(((begin + end) * (end - begin + 1)) / 2 == target){
            int[] temp = new int[end - begin + 1];
            int j = 0;
            for(int i = begin; i <= end; i++){
                temp[j++] = i;
            }
            list.add(temp);
            begin++;
            end++;
        }
    }
    return list.toArray(new int[list.size()][]);
}

58.1 ç¿»è½¬å•è¯é¡ºåº

  2. ç›´æ¥è°ƒè½¬å•è¯çš„é¡ºåºï¼Œå®šä¹‰ä¸€ä¸ªStringBufferï¼Œå®šä¹‰ä¸¤ä¸ªæŒ‡é’ˆï¼Œä»åŸæ•°ç»„æœ€åé¢å¼€å§‹å¾€å·¦æ£€ç´¢ï¼Œç›´åˆ°é‡åˆ°ç©ºæ ¼æˆ–è€…åˆ°å¤´ï¼Œæ£€ç´¢åˆ°ä¸€æ®µå•è¯ï¼Œsubstringè¿™ä¸€æ®µï¼Œæ·»åŠ åˆ°StringBufferä¸­
   // æ–¹æ³•1
public String reverseWords(String s) {
       s = s.trim();
       StringBuffer sb = new StringBuffer(s);
       sb = reverse(sb, 0, sb.length() - 1);
       int begin = 0;
       int end = 0;
       while(begin < sb.length()){
           while(end <= sb.length() -1 && sb.charAt(end) != ' '){
               end++;
           }
           sb = reverse(sb, begin, end - 1);
           begin = end;
           while(end <= sb.length() -1 && sb.charAt(end) == ' '){
               end++;
           }
           if(begin <= sb.length() -1){
               sb.replace(begin, end, String.valueOf(' '));
               begin = end - (end - begin - 1);
               end = begin;
           }
       }
       return sb.toString();
   }

   private StringBuffer reverse(StringBuffer s, int begin, int end){
       while(begin < end){
           char temp = s.charAt(begin);
           s.replace(begin,begin + 1, String.valueOf(s.charAt(end)));
           s.replace(end,end + 1, String.valueOf(temp));
           begin++;
           end--;
       }
       return s;
   }

58.2 å·¦æ—‹è½¬å­—ç¬¦ä¸²

   // æ–¹æ³•2
public String reverseLeftWords(String s, int n) {
       if(s == null || s.length() <= 0){
           return s;
       }
       if(n > s.length()){
           throw new RuntimeException();
       }
       String res = "";
       int length = s.length();
       for(int i = n; i < n + s.length(); i++){
           res += s.charAt(i % length);
       }
       return res;
   }

59.1 æ»‘åŠ¨çª—å£çš„æœ€å¤§å€¼

  2. å»ºç«‹ä¸€ä¸ªå•è°ƒé˜Ÿåˆ—ï¼Œå­˜æ”¾çª—å£ä¸­å¯èƒ½å­˜åœ¨çš„æœ€å¤§å€¼ï¼Œé‡Œé¢çš„å…ƒç´ é¡ºåºä¸ºéå•è°ƒé€’å‡ã€‚å‘å³æ»‘åŠ¨çª—å£ï¼Œè‹¥å½“å‰æ–°è¿›å…¥çª—å£çš„å…ƒç´ å¤§äºå•è°ƒé˜Ÿåˆ—å°¾éƒ¨å…ƒç´ ï¼Œåˆ™éœ€è¦åˆ é™¤é˜Ÿåˆ—å°¾éƒ¨å…ƒç´ ï¼Œè¿™ä¸ªè¿‡ç¨‹éœ€è¦å¾ªç¯ï¼Œç›´è‡³é˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸ºç©ºæˆ–è€…è¿›å…¥çª—å£çš„å…ƒç´ ä¸å¤§äºå•è°ƒé˜Ÿåˆ—å°¾éƒ¨å…ƒç´ ï¼›å°†æ–°åŠ çš„å…ƒç´ å­˜æ”¾åœ¨é˜Ÿåˆ—å°¾éƒ¨ã€‚æ³¨æ„ï¼Œè¿˜éœ€è¦åˆ¤æ–­çª—å£æ»‘åŠ¨åï¼Œå¤±å»çš„é‚£ä¸ªå…ƒç´ æ˜¯å¦æ˜¯æœ€å¤§çš„å…ƒç´ ï¼Œè‹¥æ˜¯ï¼Œåˆ™éœ€è¦åˆ é™¤é˜Ÿåˆ—å¤´éƒ¨ä¸­çš„è¯¥å…ƒç´ ã€‚
public int[] maxSlidingWindow(int[] nums, int k) {
    if(nums == null || nums.length <= 0 || k <= 0){
        int[] resExcep = new int[0];
        return resExcep;
    }
    Deque<Integer> queue = new LinkedList<>();
    for(int i = 0; i < k; i++){ //ç¬¬ä¸€ä¸ªçª—å£ï¼Œä¸ç”¨è€ƒè™‘å‰”é™¤çª—å£æ»‘åŠ¨å¤±å»çš„å…ƒç´ 
        while(queue.size() != 0 && queue.peekLast() < nums[i]){
            queue.removeLast();
        }
        queue.addLast(nums[i]);
    }
    int[] res = new int[nums.length - k + 1];
    res[0] = queue.peekFirst();
    for(int i = k; i < nums.length; i++){
        if(queue.peekFirst() == nums[i - k]){
            queue.removeFirst();
        }
        while(queue.size() != 0 && queue.peekLast() < nums[i]){
            queue.removeLast();
        }
        queue.addLast(nums[i]);
        res[i -k + 1] = queue.peekFirst();
    }
    return res;
}

59.2 é˜Ÿåˆ—çš„æœ€å¤§å€¼

é¢˜ç›®ï¼š

è¯·å®šä¹‰ä¸€ä¸ªé˜Ÿåˆ—å¹¶å®ç°å‡½æ•° max_value å¾—åˆ°é˜Ÿåˆ—é‡Œçš„æœ€å¤§å€¼ï¼Œè¦æ±‚å‡½æ•°max_valueã€push_back å’Œ pop_front çš„å‡æ‘Šæ—¶é—´å¤æ‚åº¦éƒ½æ˜¯O(1)ã€‚

è‹¥é˜Ÿåˆ—ä¸ºç©ºï¼Œpop_front å’Œ max_value éœ€è¦è¿”å› -1ã€‚

åŠ›æ‰£ï¼šç”¨ä¾‹æµ‹è¯•

æ€è·¯åˆ†æï¼š

ç±»ä¼¼ä¸Šé¢˜ï¼Œå»ºç«‹ä¸€ä¸ªå•è°ƒé˜Ÿåˆ—ï¼Œå­˜æ”¾å¯èƒ½å­˜åœ¨çš„æœ€å¤§å€¼ã€‚

private LinkedList<Integer> max;
private LinkedList<Integer> list;

public MaxQueue() {
    max = new LinkedList<>();
    list = new LinkedList<>();
}

public int max_value() {   
    return max.size() == 0 ? -1 : max.getFirst();
}

public void push_back(int value) {
    list.addLast(value);
    while(max.size() != 0 && max.getLast() < value){
        max.removeLast();
    }
    max.addLast(value);
}

public int pop_front() {
    if(list.size() == 0)    return -1;
    int res = list.getFirst();
    if(max.getFirst() == res){
        max.removeFirst();
    }
    list.removeFirst();
    return res;
}

åŠ¨æ€è§„åˆ’ã€‚ n ä¸ªéª°å­å¯ä»¥åˆ†ä¸º n - 1 ä¸ªéª°å­å’Œ 1 ä¸ªéª°å­ç»„åˆã€‚é¦–å…ˆï¼Œn ä¸ªéª°å­ï¼Œå¯èƒ½çš„ç‚¹æ•°ä¸ªæ•°ä¸º 5 * n + 1ã€‚n - 1ä¸ªéª°å­å’Œ 1 ä¸ªéª°å­ç»„åˆä¸­çš„ 1 ä¸ªéª°å­ï¼Œæ¦‚ç‡æ˜¯å›ºå®šçš„ï¼Œ6ä¸ªå…ƒç´ æ¦‚ç‡å‡ä¸º 1 / 6ï¼›n - 1 ä¸ªéª°å­å’Œ 1 ä¸ªéª°å­ç»„åˆï¼Œå°±æ˜¯ä»–ä»¬çš„å…ƒç´ ä¸¤ä¸¤ç›¸ä¹˜ã€‚

public double[] twoSum(int n) {
    if(n <= 0){
        throw new RuntimeException();
    }
    double[] pre = {1/6d,1/6d,1/6d,1/6d,1/6d,1/6d}; // n - 1 ä¸ªéª°å­
    for(int i = 2; i <= n; i++){
        double[] later = new double[5 * i + 1];  // n ä¸ªéª°å­
        for(int j = 0; j < pre.length; j++){
            for(int k = 0; k < 6; k++){
                later[k + j] += pre[j] / 6d;  // n - 1 ä¸ªéª°å­å’Œ 1 ä¸ªéª°å­ç»„åˆå¾—åˆ° n ä¸ªéª°å­ç»“æœ
            }
        }
        pre = later;
    }
    return pre;
}

61ã€æ‰‘å…‹ç‰Œä¸­çš„é¡ºå­

ä»æ‰‘å…‹ç‰Œä¸­éšæœºæŠ½5å¼ ç‰Œï¼Œåˆ¤æ–­æ˜¯ä¸æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªé¡ºå­ï¼Œå³è¿™5å¼ ç‰Œæ˜¯ä¸æ˜¯è¿ç»­çš„ã€‚2ï½10ä¸ºæ•°å­—æœ¬èº«ï¼ŒAä¸º1ï¼ŒJä¸º11ï¼ŒQä¸º12ï¼ŒKä¸º13ï¼Œè€Œå¤§ã€å°ç‹ä¸º 0 ï¼Œå¯ä»¥çœ‹æˆä»»æ„æ•°å­—ã€‚A ä¸èƒ½è§†ä¸º 14ã€‚

åŠ›æ‰£ï¼šç”¨ä¾‹æµ‹è¯•

æ€è·¯åˆ†æï¼š

å¤§ç‹å°ç‹ä¸º 0ï¼Œå…¶ä½™ç‰Œä¸º 1~13ã€‚åŒæ—¶æ»¡è¶³ä»¥ä¸‹ä¸¤ä¸ªæ¡ä»¶ï¼Œ5å¼ æ‰‘å…‹ç‰Œæ„æˆé¡ºå­ã€‚

  1. é™¤ 0 å¤–ï¼Œæ— é‡å¤ç‰Œï¼›
  2. ç‰Œä¸­æœ€å¤§çš„æ•°å­—å‡å»æœ€å°çš„æ•°å­— < 5ã€‚
public boolean isStraight(int[] nums) {
    if(nums == null || nums.length == 0){
        return false;
    }
    Set<Integer> set = new HashSet<>();
    int max = 0;
    int min = 20;
    for(int num : nums){
        if(num == 0){
            continue;
        }
        if(set.contains(num)){
            return false;
        }
        max = Math.max(max,num);
        min = Math.min(min,num);
        set.add(num);
    }
    return max - min < 5;
}

public int lastRemaining(int n, int m) {
    if(n <= 0 || m <= 0){
        throw new RuntimeException();
    }
    int res = 0;
    for(int i = 2; i <= n; i++){
        res = (res + m) % i;
    }
    return res;
}

public int maxProfit(int[] prices) {
    if(prices == null || prices.length <= 1){
        return 0;
    }
    int pre = 0;
    int later = 0;
    int min = prices[0];
    for(int i = 1; i < prices.length; i++){
        pre = later;
        min = Math.min(min, prices[i]);
        later = Math.max(pre, prices[i] - min);
    }
    return later;
}

public int add(int a, int b) {
    int c = 0;  // è¿›ä½ä¿¡æ¯
    while(b != 0){
        c = (a & b) << 1;
        a = a ^ b;  // ä¸åšè¿›ä½çš„ç»“æœ
        b = c;
    }
    return a;
}

66ã€æ„å»ºä¹˜ç§¯æ•°ç»„

ç»™å®šä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ A[0,1,â€¦,n-1]ï¼Œè¯·æ„å»ºä¸€ä¸ªæ•°ç»„ B[0,1,â€¦,n-1]ï¼Œå…¶ä¸­ B ä¸­çš„å…ƒç´  B[i]=A[0]Ã—A[1]Ã—â€¦Ã—A[i-1]Ã—A[i+1]Ã—â€¦Ã—A[n-1]ã€‚ä¸èƒ½ä½¿ç”¨é™¤æ³•ã€‚

public int[] constructArr(int[] a) {
    if(a == null || a.length <= 0){
        return new int[0];
    }
    int[] b = new int[a.length];
    b[0] = 1;
    for(int i = 1; i < a.length; i++){
        b[i] = b[i - 1] * a[i - 1];
    }
    int temp = 1;
    for(int i = a.length - 2; i >=0; i--){
        temp *= a[i + 1];
        b[i] *= temp;
    }
    return b;
}

å‡è®¾æˆ‘ä»¬çš„ç¯å¢ƒåªèƒ½å­˜å‚¨ 32 ä½å¤§å°çš„æœ‰ç¬¦å·æ•´æ•°ï¼Œé‚£ä¹ˆå…¶æ•°å€¼èŒƒå›´ä¸º [âˆ’231, 231 âˆ’ 1]ã€‚å¦‚æœæ•°å€¼è¶…è¿‡è¿™ä¸ªèŒƒå›´ï¼Œè¯·è¿”å› INT_MAX (231 âˆ’ 1) æˆ– INT_MIN (âˆ’231) ã€‚

public int strToInt(String str) {
    if(str == null || str.length() <= 0){
        return 0;
    }
    int index = 0;
    int sign = 1; // æ­£è´Ÿå·
    int max = Integer.MAX_VALUE;
    int res = 0;
    while(str.charAt(index) == ' '){
        if(++index == str.length()){
            return 0;
        }
    } // å»é™¤å¤´éƒ¨ç©ºæ ¼
    if(str.charAt(index) == '-'){
        sign = -1;
    }
    if(str.charAt(index) == '+' || str.charAt(index) == '-'){
        index++;
    } // æ£€ç´¢æ­£è´Ÿå·
    for(; index < str.length(); index++){
        if(str.charAt(index) < '0' || str.charAt(index) > '9'){
            break;
        }
        if(res > max / 10 || (res == max / 10 && str.charAt(index) > '7')){
            return sign == 1 ? max : Integer.MIN_VALUE;
        }
        res = res * 10 + (str.charAt(index) - '0');
    }
    return sign * res;
}

åŠ›æ‰£ï¼šç”¨ä¾‹æµ‹è¯•

æ€è·¯åˆ†æï¼š

äºŒå‰æœç´¢æ ‘ï¼Œä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å·¦å­æ ‘ä¸­æ‰€æœ‰èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å€¼å®ƒçš„å€¼å°ï¼Œå³å­æ ‘ä¸­æ‰€æœ‰èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å€¼å®ƒçš„å€¼å¤§ã€‚å¯¹äºè¾“å…¥çš„ä¸¤ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹ï¼Œè‹¥æ‰¾åˆ°ä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å€¼ï¼Œä»‹äºè¿™ä¸¤ä¸ªä¹‹é—´ï¼Œåˆ™æ‰¾åˆ°ç›®æ ‡èŠ‚ç‚¹ã€‚è‹¥ä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å€¼å¤§äºè¿™ä¸¤ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å€¼ï¼Œåˆ™éœ€è¦åœ¨è¯¥èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å·¦å­èŠ‚ç‚¹ç»§ç»­å¯»æ‰¾ï¼›è‹¥ä¸€ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å€¼å°äºè¿™ä¸¤ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å€¼ï¼Œåˆ™éœ€è¦åœ¨è¯¥èŠ‚ç‚¹çš„å³å­èŠ‚ç‚¹ç»§ç»­å¯»æ‰¾.

public TreeNode lowestCommonAncestor(TreeNode root, TreeNode p, TreeNode q) {
    while(root != null){
        if(root.val > p.val && root.val > q.val){
            root = root.left;
        }else if(root.val < p.val && root.val < q.val){
            root = root.right;
        }else{
            break;
        }
    }
    return root;
}

68.2 äºŒå‰æ ‘çš„æœ€è¿‘å…¬å…±ç¥–å…ˆ

é¢˜ç›®ï¼š

ç»™å®šä¸€ä¸ªäºŒå‰æ ‘, æ‰¾åˆ°è¯¥æ ‘ä¸­ä¸¤ä¸ªæŒ‡å®šèŠ‚ç‚¹çš„æœ€è¿‘å…¬å…±ç¥–å…ˆã€‚

åŠ›æ‰£ï¼šç”¨ä¾‹æµ‹è¯•

æ€è·¯åˆ†æï¼š

  1. p å’Œ q åœ¨ root çš„å­æ ‘ä¸­ï¼Œä¸”åˆ†åˆ— rootroot çš„ å¼‚ä¾§ï¼ˆå³åˆ†åˆ«åœ¨å·¦ã€å³å­æ ‘ä¸­ï¼‰ï¼›

  2. p = root ï¼Œä¸” q åœ¨ root çš„å·¦æˆ–å³å­æ ‘ä¸­ï¼›

  3. q = root ï¼Œä¸” p åœ¨ root çš„å·¦æˆ–å³å­æ ‘ä¸­ã€‚

ä¸æ–­é€’å½’ã€‚

public TreeNode lowestCommonAncestor(TreeNode root, TreeNode p, TreeNode q) {
    if(root == null || root == p || root == q){
        return root;
    }
    TreeNode left = lowestCommonAncestor(root.left, p, q);
    TreeNode right = lowestCommonAncestor(root.right, p, q);
    if(left == null && right == null){
        return null;
    }
    if(left == null){
        return right;
    }
    if(right == null){
        return left;
    }
    return root;
}
